##### **Is There Knowledge Left to Extract? Evidence of Fragility in Medically Fine-Tuned Vision-Language Models**
2604.09841v1 by Oliver McLaughlin, Daniel Shubin, Carsten Eickhoff, Ritambhara Singh, William Rudman, Michal Golovanevsky

Vision-language models (VLMs) are increasingly adapted through domain-specific fine-tuning, yet it remains unclear whether this improves reasoning beyond superficial visual cues, particularly in high-stakes domains like medicine. We evaluate four paired open-source VLMs (LLaVA vs. LLaVA-Med; Gemma vs. MedGemma) across four medical imaging tasks of increasing difficulty: brain tumor, pneumonia, skin cancer, and histopathology classification. We find that performance degrades toward near-random levels as task difficulty increases, indicating limited clinical reasoning. Medical fine-tuning provides no consistent advantage, and models are highly sensitive to prompt formulation, with minor changes causing large swings in accuracy and refusal rates. To test whether closed-form VQA suppresses latent knowledge, we introduce a description-based pipeline where models generate image descriptions that a text-only model (GPT-5.1) uses for diagnosis. This recovers a limited additional signal but remains bounded by task difficulty. Analysis of vision encoder embeddings further shows that failures stem from both weak visual representations and downstream reasoning. Overall, medical VLM performance is fragile, prompt-dependent, and not reliably improved by domain-specific fine-tuning.

摘要：視覺-語言模型（VLMs）越來越多地通過特定領域的微調進行調整，但尚不清楚這是否能改善推理能力，超越表面的視覺線索，特別是在像醫學這樣的高風險領域。我們評估了四對開源VLM（LLaVA與LLaVA-Med；Gemma與MedGemma）在四個逐漸增加難度的醫學影像任務中的表現：腦腫瘤、肺炎、皮膚癌和組織病理學分類。我們發現，隨著任務難度的增加，表現會降至接近隨機的水平，這表明臨床推理能力有限。醫學微調並未提供一致的優勢，模型對提示的表述高度敏感，輕微的變化會導致準確率和拒絕率的大幅波動。為了測試封閉形式的VQA是否抑制潛在知識，我們引入了一個基於描述的流程，模型生成的圖像描述供一個僅文本模型（GPT-5.1）用於診斷。這恢復了一定的額外信號，但仍然受到任務難度的限制。對視覺編碼器嵌入的分析進一步顯示，失敗源於弱視覺表徵和下游推理的問題。總體而言，醫學VLM的表現脆弱，依賴於提示，並且不會因特定領域的微調而可靠地改善。

##### **Process Reward Agents for Steering Knowledge-Intensive Reasoning**
2604.09482v1 by Jiwoong Sohn, Tomasz Sternal, Kenneth Styppa, Torsten Hoefler, Michael Moor

Reasoning in knowledge-intensive domains remains challenging as intermediate steps are often not locally verifiable: unlike math or code, evaluating step correctness may require synthesizing clues across large external knowledge sources. As a result, subtle errors can propagate through reasoning traces, potentially never to be detected. Prior work has proposed process reward models (PRMs), including retrieval-augmented variants, but these methods operate post hoc, scoring completed trajectories, which prevents their integration into dynamic inference procedures. Here, we introduce Process Reward Agents (PRA), a test-time method for providing domain-grounded, online, step-wise rewards to a frozen policy. In contrast to prior retrieval-augmented PRMs, PRA enables search-based decoding to rank and prune candidate trajectories at every generation step. Experiments on multiple medical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PRA consistently outperforms strong baselines, achieving 80.8% accuracy on MedQA with Qwen3-4B, a new state of the art at the 4B scale. Importantly, PRA generalizes to unseen frozen policy models ranging from 0.5B to 8B parameters, improving their accuracy by up to 25.7% without any policy model updates. More broadly, PRA suggests a paradigm in which frozen reasoners are decoupled from domain-specific reward modules, allowing the deployment of new backbones in complex domains without retraining.

摘要：知識密集型領域的推理仍然具有挑戰性，因為中間步驟往往無法在本地驗證：與數學或程式碼不同，評估步驟的正確性可能需要綜合來自大型外部知識來源的線索。結果，微妙的錯誤可能會在推理過程中傳播，潛在地永遠無法被檢測到。先前的研究提出了過程獎勵模型（PRMs），包括檢索增強變體，但這些方法是在事後運作，對已完成的軌跡進行評分，這阻礙了它們在動態推理程序中的整合。在這裡，我們介紹了過程獎勵代理（PRA），這是一種在測試時提供基於領域的、在線的、逐步獎勵給冷凍策略的方法。與先前的檢索增強PRMs相比，PRA使基於搜索的解碼能夠在每個生成步驟中對候選軌跡進行排名和修剪。在多個醫療推理基準上的實驗表明，PRA始終超越強基線，在MedQA上以Qwen3-4B達到80.8%的準確率，這是4B規模的新最先進技術。重要的是，PRA能夠推廣到未見過的冷凍策略模型，參數範圍從0.5B到8B，將其準確性提高了多達25.7%，而無需任何策略模型更新。更廣泛地說，PRA提出了一種範式，其中冷凍推理器與特定領域的獎勵模塊解耦，允許在複雜領域中部署新的骨幹而無需重新訓練。

##### **ECHO: Efficient Chest X-ray Report Generation with One-step Block Diffusion**
2604.09450v1 by Lifeng Chen, Tianqi You, Hao Liu, Zhimin Bao, Jile Jiao, Xiao Han, Zhicai Ou, Tao Sun, Xiaofeng Mou, Xiaojie Jin, Yi Xu

Chest X-ray report generation (CXR-RG) has the potential to substantially alleviate radiologists' workload. However, conventional autoregressive vision--language models (VLMs) suffer from high inference latency due to sequential token decoding. Diffusion-based models offer a promising alternative through parallel generation, but they still require multiple denoising iterations. Compressing multi-step denoising to a single step could further reduce latency, but often degrades textual coherence due to the mean-field bias introduced by token-factorized denoisers. To address this challenge, we propose \textbf{ECHO}, an efficient diffusion-based VLM (dVLM) for chest X-ray report generation. ECHO enables stable one-step-per-block inference via a novel Direct Conditional Distillation (DCD) framework, which mitigates the mean-field limitation by constructing unfactorized supervision from on-policy diffusion trajectories to encode joint token dependencies. In addition, we introduce a Response-Asymmetric Diffusion (RAD) training strategy that further improves training efficiency while maintaining model effectiveness. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ECHO surpasses state-of-the-art autoregressive methods, improving RaTE and SemScore by \textbf{64.33\%} and \textbf{60.58\%} respectively, while achieving an \textbf{$8\times$} inference speedup without compromising clinical accuracy.

摘要：胸部X光報告生成（CXR-RG）有潛力顯著減輕放射科醫師的工作負擔。<lb/>然而，傳統的自回歸視覺-語言模型（VLMs）因為序列標記解碼而遭受高推理延遲。<lb/>基於擴散的模型透過平行生成提供了一個有希望的替代方案，但仍然需要多次去噪迭代。<lb/>將多步驟去噪壓縮為單一步驟可以進一步減少延遲，但通常會因為標記分解去噪器引入的均場偏差而降低文本一致性。<lb/>為了解決這一挑戰，我們提出了\textbf{ECHO}，一種高效的基於擴散的VLM（dVLM）用於胸部X光報告生成。<lb/>ECHO通過一個新穎的直接條件蒸餾（DCD）框架實現穩定的每區塊一步推理，該框架通過從政策擴散軌跡構建未分解的監督來緩解均場限制，以編碼聯合標記依賴性。<lb/>此外，我們還引入了一種反應不對稱擴散（RAD）訓練策略，進一步提高訓練效率，同時保持模型的有效性。<lb/>大量實驗表明，ECHO超越了最先進的自回歸方法，RaTE和SemScore分別提高了\textbf{64.33\%}和\textbf{60.58\%}，同時在不妥協臨床準確性的情況下實現了\textbf{$8\times$}的推理加速。

##### **MedLVR: Latent Visual Reasoning for Reliable Medical Visual Question Answering**
2604.09757v1 by Suyang Xi, Songtao Hu, Yuxiang Lai, Wangyun Dan, Yaqi Liu, Shansong Wang, Xiaofeng Yang

Medical vision--language models (VLMs) have shown strong potential for medical visual question answering (VQA), yet their reasoning remains largely text-centric: images are encoded once as static context, and subsequent inference is dominated by language. This paradigm is fundamentally limited in clinical scenarios, where accurate answers often depend on subtle, localized visual evidence that cannot be reliably preserved in static embeddings. We propose \textsc{MedLVR}, a latent visual reasoning framework that introduces an explicit visual evidence state into autoregressive decoding. Instead of relying solely on text-based intermediate reasoning, \textsc{MedLVR} interleaves a short latent reasoning segment within the decoder by reusing hidden states as continuous latent steps, enabling iterative preservation and refinement of query-relevant visual evidence before answer generation. To support effective visual supervision, we adopt a two-stage training strategy: region of interest (ROI)-supervised fine-tuning aligns latent states with clinically relevant image evidence, and Visual-Latent Policy Optimization (VLPO) further optimizes latent reasoning and answer generation under outcome-level rewards. Experiments on OmniMedVQA and five external medical VQA benchmarks show that \textsc{MedLVR} consistently outperforms recent reasoning baselines and improves the average score over the Qwen2.5-VL-7B backbone from 48.3\% to 53.4\%. These results show that latent visual reasoning provides an effective mechanism for preserving diagnostically relevant visual evidence and improving the reliability of medical VQA.

摘要：醫療視覺-語言模型（VLMs）在醫療視覺問題回答（VQA）中顯示出強大的潛力，但它們的推理仍然主要以文本為中心：圖像被一次性編碼為靜態上下文，隨後的推理則以語言為主導。這種範式在臨床場景中基本上是有限的，因為準確的答案往往依賴於微妙的、局部的視覺證據，而這些證據無法在靜態嵌入中可靠地保留。我們提出了\textsc{MedLVR}，一種潛在視覺推理框架，將明確的視覺證據狀態引入自回歸解碼中。\textsc{MedLVR}不僅依賴於基於文本的中間推理，而是在解碼器中交錯一段短的潛在推理片段，通過重用隱藏狀態作為連續的潛在步驟，使得在生成答案之前能夠迭代地保留和精煉與查詢相關的視覺證據。為了支持有效的視覺監督，我們採用兩階段的訓練策略：感興趣區域（ROI）監督的微調將潛在狀態與臨床相關的圖像證據對齊，而視覺-潛在策略優化（VLPO）進一步在結果層級獎勵下優化潛在推理和答案生成。在OmniMedVQA和五個外部醫療VQA基準上的實驗顯示，\textsc{MedLVR}始終超越最近的推理基線，並將Qwen2.5-VL-7B骨幹的平均分數從48.3\%提高到53.4\%。這些結果表明，潛在視覺推理提供了一種有效的機制來保留診斷相關的視覺證據並提高醫療VQA的可靠性。

##### **The Fast Lane Hypothesis: Von Economo Neurons Implement a Biological Speed-Accuracy Tradeoff**
2604.09229v1 by Esila Keskin

Von Economo neurons (VENs) are large bipolar projection neurons found exclusively in the anterior cingulate cortex (ACC) and frontal insula of species with complex social cognition, including humans, great apes, and cetaceans. Their selective depletion in frontotemporal dementia (FTD) and altered development in autism implicate them in rapid social decision-making, yet no computational model of VEN function has previously existed. We introduce the Fast Lane Hypothesis: VENs implement a biological speed-accuracy tradeoff (SAT) by providing a sparse, fast projection pathway that enables rapid social decisions at the cost of deliberate processing accuracy. We model VENs as fast leaky integrate-and-fire (LIF) neurons with membrane time constant 5 ms and sparse dendritic fan-in of eight afferents, compared to 20 ms and eighty afferents for standard pyramidal neurons, within a spiking cortical circuit of 2,000 neurons trained on a social discrimination task. Networks are evaluated under three clinically motivated conditions across 10 independent random seeds: typical (2% VENs), autism-like (0.4% VENs), and FTD-like (post-training VEN ablation). All configurations achieve equivalent asymptotic classification accuracy (99.4%), consistent with the prediction that VENs modulate decision speed rather than representational capacity. Temporal analysis confirms that VENs produce median first-spike latencies 4 ms earlier than pyramidal neurons. At a fixed decision threshold, the typical condition is significantly faster than FTD-like (t=-23.31, p<0.0001), while autism-like is intermediate (mean RT=26.91+/-9.01 ms vs. typical 20.70+/-2.02 ms; p=0.078). A preliminary evolutionary analysis shows qualitative correspondence between model-optimal VEN fraction and the primate phylogenetic gradient. To our knowledge, this is the first computational model that asks what a Von Economo neuron actually computes.

摘要：Von Economo 神經元 (VENs) 是一種大型雙極性投射神經元，僅存在於具有複雜社會認知的物種的前扣帶皮質 (ACC) 和額葉島，包括人類、大猩猩和鯨類。<lb/>它們在額顳癡呆症 (FTD) 中的選擇性耗竭以及在自閉症中的發展變化，使它們與快速社會決策相關聯，但之前並不存在 VEN 功能的計算模型。<lb/>我們提出了快速通道假說：VENs 通過提供稀疏、快速的投射通路來實現生物學上的速度-準確性權衡 (SAT)，這使得快速社會決策的代價是深思熟慮的處理準確性。<lb/>我們將 VENs 模型化為快速漏積-發火 (LIF) 神經元，膜時間常數為 5 毫秒，稀疏的樹突進入為八個傳入神經元，相較於標準錐體神經元的 20 毫秒和八十個傳入神經元，這是在一個包含 2,000 個神經元的尖峰皮質電路中訓練於社會辨別任務。<lb/>在 10 個獨立隨機種子下，網絡在三個臨床動機的條件下進行評估：典型 (2% VENs)、類自閉症 (0.4% VENs) 和類 FTD (訓練後 VEN 切除)。<lb/>所有配置達到相當的漸近分類準確率 (99.4%)，這與 VENs 調節決策速度而非表徵能力的預測一致。<lb/>時間分析確認 VENs 產生的中位首次尖峰潛伏期比錐體神經元早 4 毫秒。<lb/>在固定的決策閾值下，典型條件顯著快於類 FTD (t=-23.31, p&lt;0.0001)，而類自閉症則居中 (平均反應時間=26.91+/-9.01 毫秒對比典型的 20.70+/-2.02 毫秒; p=0.078)。<lb/>初步的進化分析顯示模型最佳 VEN 比例與靈長類動物的系統發育梯度之間存在定性對應。<lb/>據我們所知，這是第一個計算模型，詢問 Von Economo 神經元實際計算了什麼。

摘要：目的。高級漿液性卵巢癌（HGSOC）以明顯的生物學和空間異質性為特徵，並且經常在晚期被診斷。對於不適合進行初次細胞減少術的患者，通常採用新輔助化療（NACT）後延遲的主要手術。化療反應評分（CRS）是一種經過驗證的組織病理學生物標記，用於評估對NACT的反應，但僅在手術後可用。在本研究中，我們探討了是否可以使用治療前的計算機斷層掃描（CT）影像和臨床數據來預測CRS，作為一種研究性決策支持輔助工具，以通知多學科團隊（MDT）討論預期的治療反應。方法。我們提出了一種2.5D多模態深度學習框架，該框架使用預訓練的視覺Transformer編碼器處理病灶密集的網膜切片，並通過中間融合模塊將生成的視覺表示與臨床變量整合，以預測CRS。結果。我們的多模態模型整合了影像和臨床數據，在內部測試隊列（IEO，n=41名患者）中達到了0.95的ROC-AUC，以及95%的準確率和80%的精確度。在外部測試集（OV04，n=70名患者）中，它達到了0.68的ROC-AUC，以及67%的準確率和75%的精確度。結論。這些初步結果顯示，基於Transformer的深度學習在使用常規臨床數據和CT影像進行HGSOC的術前CRS預測方面是可行的。作為一種研究性、治療前的決策支持工具，這種方法可能通過提供早期、非侵入性的治療反應估計來協助MDT討論。

##### **Adaptive Dual Residual U-Net with Attention Gate and Multiscale Spatial Attention Mechanisms (ADRUwAMS)**
2604.08893v1 by Mohsen Yaghoubi Suraki

Glioma is a harmful brain tumor that requires early detection to ensure better health results. Early detection of this tumor is key for effective treatment and requires an automated segmentation process. However, it is a challenging task to find tumors due to tumor characteristics like location and size. A reliable method to accurately separate tumor zones from healthy tissues is deep learning models, which have shown promising results over the last few years. In this research, an Adaptive Dual Residual U-Net with Attention Gate and Multiscale Spatial Attention Mechanisms (ADRUwAMS) is introduced. This model is an innovative combination of adaptive dual residual networks, attention mechanisms, and multiscale spatial attention. The dual adaptive residual network architecture captures high-level semantic and intricate low-level details from brain images, ensuring precise segmentation of different tumor parts, types, and hard regions. The attention gates use gating and input signals to compute attention coefficients for the input features, and multiscale spatial attention generates scaled attention maps and combines these features to hold the most significant information about the brain tumor. We trained the model for 200 epochs using the ReLU activation function on BraTS 2020 and BraTS 2019 datasets. 摘要：膠質瘤是一種有害的腦腫瘤，需要及早檢測以確保更好的健康結果。這種腫瘤的早期檢測對於有效治療至關重要，並且需要自動分割過程。然而，由於腫瘤的特徵，如位置和大小，找到腫瘤是一項具有挑戰性的任務。一種可靠的方法是使用深度學習模型，準確地將腫瘤區域與健康組織分開，這在過去幾年中已顯示出良好的結果。在這項研究中，介紹了一種具有注意力閘和多尺度空間注意機制的自適應雙殘差 U-Net（ADRUwAMS）。這個模型是自適應雙殘差網絡、注意力機制和多尺度空間注意的創新組合。雙自適應殘差網絡架構從腦部圖像中捕捉高級語義和複雜的低級細節，確保不同腫瘤部分、類型和困難區域的精確分割。注意力閘使用閘控和輸入信號計算輸入特徵的注意力係數，而多尺度空間注意生成縮放的注意力圖並結合這些特徵以保留有關腦腫瘤的最重要信息。我們在 BraTS 2020 和 BraTS 2019 數據集上使用 ReLU 激活函數訓練模型 200 個時期。這些改進使得在 BraTS 2020 上的腫瘤檢測和分割達到了高準確率，整個腫瘤的 dice 分數為 0.9229，腫瘤核心為 0.8432，增強腫瘤為 0.8004。

##### **MedFormer-UR: Uncertainty-Routed Transformer for Medical Image Classification**
2604.08868v1 by Mohammed Maaz Sibhai, Abedalrhman Alkhateeb, Saad B. Ahmed

To ensure safe clinical integration, deep learning models must provide more than just high accuracy; they require dependable uncertainty quantification. While current Medical Vision Transformers perform well, they frequently struggle with overconfident predictions and a lack of transparency, issues that are magnified by the noisy and imbalanced nature of clinical data. To address this, we enhanced the modified Medical Transformer (MedFormer) that incorporates prototype-based learning and uncertainty-guided routing, by utilizing a Dirichlet distribution for per-token evidential uncertainty, our framework can quantify and localize ambiguity in real-time. This uncertainty is not just an output but an active participant in the training process, filtering out unreliable feature updates. Furthermore, the use of class-specific prototypes ensures the embedding space remains structured, allowing for decisions based on visual similarity. 摘要：為了確保安全的臨床整合，深度學習模型必須提供的不僅僅是高準確度；它們還需要可靠的不確定性量化。雖然當前的醫療視覺Transformer表現良好，但它們經常在過度自信的預測和缺乏透明度方面遇到困難，這些問題因臨床數據的噪聲和不平衡性而加劇。為了解決這個問題，我們增強了修改後的醫療Transformer（MedFormer），該Transformer結合了基於原型的學習和不確定性引導的路由，通過利用Dirichlet分佈來獲取每個標記的證據不確定性，我們的框架可以實時量化和定位模糊性。這種不確定性不僅僅是一個輸出，而是訓練過程中的一個積極參與者，過濾掉不可靠的特徵更新。此外，使用類別特定的原型確保了嵌入空間保持結構化，允許基於視覺相似性做出決策。在四種模態（乳腺攝影、超聲波、MRI和組織病理學）上的測試證實，我們的方法顯著增強了模型的校準，將預期校準誤差（ECE）降低了多達35%，並改善了選擇性預測，即使在準確度增益較小的情況下。

##### **Scalable High-Recall Constraint-Satisfaction-Based Information Retrieval for Clinical Trials Matching**
2604.08849v1 by Cyrus Zhou, Yufei Jin, Yilin Xu, Yu-Chiang Wang, Chieh-Ju Chao, Monica S. Lam

Clinical trials are central to evidence-based medicine, yet many struggle to meet enrollment targets, despite the availability of over half a million trials listed on ClinicalTrials.gov, which attracts approximately two million users monthly. Existing retrieval techniques, largely based on keyword and embedding-similarity matching between patient profiles and eligibility criteria, often struggle with low recall, low precision, and limited interpretability due to complex constraints. We propose SatIR, a scalable clinical trial retrieval method based on constraint satisfaction, enabling high-precision and interpretable matching of patients to relevant trials. Our approach uses formal methods -- Satisfiability Modulo Theories (SMT) and relational algebra -- to efficiently represent and match key constraints from clinical trials and patient records. Beyond leveraging established medical ontologies and conceptual models, we use Large Language Models (LLMs) to convert informal reasoning regarding ambiguity, implicit clinical assumptions, and incomplete patient records into explicit, precise, controllable, and interpretable formal constraints. Evaluated on 59 patients and 3,621 trials, SatIR outperforms TrialGPT on all three evaluated retrieval objectives. It retrieves 32%-72% more relevant-and-eligible trials per patient, improves recall over the union of useful trials by 22-38 points, and serves more patients with at least one useful trial. Retrieval is fast, requiring 2.95 seconds per patient over 3,621 trials. These results show that SatIR is scalable, effective, and interpretable.

摘要：臨床試驗是循證醫學的核心，但儘管 ClinicalTrials.gov 上列出了超過五十萬個試驗，每月吸引約兩百萬用戶，許多試驗仍然難以達到招募目標。現有的檢索技術主要基於關鍵字和患者檔案與資格標準之間的嵌入相似度匹配，往往面臨低召回率、低精確度和由於複雜約束導致的有限可解釋性問題。我們提出了 SatIR，一種基於約束滿足的可擴展臨床試驗檢索方法，能夠高精度和可解釋地將患者與相關試驗匹配。我們的方法使用形式化方法——滿足性模組理論（SMT）和關係代數——來有效地表示和匹配臨床試驗和患者記錄中的關鍵約束。除了利用既有的醫學本體論和概念模型外，我們還使用大型語言模型（LLMs）將有關模糊性、隱含臨床假設和不完整患者記錄的非正式推理轉換為明確、精確、可控和可解釋的形式約束。在對59名患者和3,621個試驗進行評估後，SatIR 在所有三個評估的檢索目標上均優於 TrialGPT。它每位患者檢索到的相關且符合資格的試驗多出32%-72%，在有用試驗的聯集上提高了22-38個點的召回率，並為更多患者提供至少一個有用的試驗。檢索速度快，對每位患者在3,621個試驗中僅需2.95秒。這些結果表明，SatIR 是可擴展的、有效的和可解釋的。

##### **STaR-DRO: Stateful Tsallis Reweighting for Group-Robust Structured Prediction**
2604.09737v1 by Samah Fodeh, Ganesh Puthiaraju, Elyas Irankhah, Linhai Ma, Srivani Talakokkul, Afshan Khan, Sreeraj Ramachandran, Jordan Alpert, Sarah Schellhorn

Structured prediction requires models to generate ontology-constrained labels, grounded evidence, and valid structure under ambiguity, label skew, and heterogeneous group difficulty. We present a two-part framework for controllable inference and robust fine-tuning. First, we introduce a task-agnostic prompting strategy that combines XML-based instruction structure, disambiguation rules, verification-style reasoning, schema constraints, and self-validation to address format drift, label ambiguity, evidence hallucination, and metadata-conditioned confusion in in-context structured generation. Second, we introduce STaR-DRO, a stateful robust optimization method for group heterogeneity. It combines Tsallis mirror descent with momentum-smoothed, centered group-loss signals and bounded excess-only multipliers so that only persistently hard groups above a neutral baseline are upweighted, concentrating learning where it is most needed while avoiding volatile, dense exponentiated-gradient reweighting and unnecessary loss from downweighting easier groups. We evaluate the combined framework on EPPC Miner, a benchmark for extracting hierarchical labels and evidence spans from patient-provider secure messages. Prompt engineering improves zero-shot by +15.44 average F1 across Code, Sub-code, and Span over four Llama models. Building on supervised fine-tuning, STaR-DRO further improves the hardest semantic decisions: on Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct, Code F1 rises from 79.24 to 81.47 and Sub-code F1 from 67.78 to 69.30, while preserving Span performance and reducing group-wise validation cross-entropy by up to 29.6% on the most difficult clinical categories. Because these rare and difficult groups correspond to clinically consequential communication behaviors, these gains are not merely statistical improvements: they directly strengthen communication mining reliability for patient-centered care analysis.

摘要：結構化預測要求模型在模糊性、標籤偏差和異質性群體困難下生成受本體約束的標籤、基於證據的內容和有效結構。我們提出了一個由兩部分組成的框架，用於可控推理和穩健的微調。首先，我們介紹了一種與任務無關的提示策略，該策略結合了基於XML的指令結構、消歧規則、驗證式推理、模式約束和自我驗證，以解決上下文結構生成中的格式漂移、標籤模糊、證據幻覺和元數據條件混淆。其次，我們介紹了STaR-DRO，一種針對群體異質性的有狀態穩健優化方法。它結合了Tsallis鏡像下降與動量平滑的集中群體損失信號和有界的超額乘子，這樣只有持續困難的群體在中性基準之上被加權，提高學習集中在最需要的地方，同時避免不穩定的、密集的指數梯度重加權和因降低較易群體權重而產生的不必要損失。我們在EPPC Miner上評估了這個綜合框架，該基準用於從患者與提供者的安全消息中提取層次標籤和證據範圍。提示工程使得零樣本的平均F1在四個Llama模型上提高了+15.44，涵蓋了代碼、子代碼和範圍。在監督微調的基礎上，STaR-DRO進一步改善了最困難的語義決策：在Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct上，代碼F1從79.24上升到81.47，子代碼F1從67.78上升到69.30，同時保持範圍性能並將最困難臨床類別的群體驗證交叉熵降低了多達29.6%。因為這些稀有且困難的群體與臨床上重要的溝通行為相對應，這些增益不僅僅是統計上的改善：它們直接增強了以患者為中心的護理分析中的溝通挖掘可靠性。

##### **Quantifying Explanation Consistency: The C-Score Metric for CAM-Based Explainability in Medical Image Classification**
2604.08502v1 by Kabilan Elangovan, Daniel Ting

Class Activation Mapping (CAM) methods are widely used to generate visual explanations for deep learning classifiers in medical imaging. However, existing evaluation frameworks assess whether explanations are correct, measured by localisation fidelity against radiologist annotations, rather than whether they are consistent: whether the model applies the same spatial reasoning strategy across different patients with the same pathology. We propose the C-Score (Consistency Score), a confidence-weighted, annotation-free metric that quantifies intra-class explanation reproducibility via intensity-emphasised pairwise soft IoU across correctly classified instances. We evaluate six CAM techniques: GradCAM, GradCAM++, LayerCAM, EigenCAM, ScoreCAM, and MS GradCAM++ across three CNN architectures (DenseNet201, InceptionV3, ResNet50V2) over thirty training epochs on the Kermany chest X-ray dataset, covering transfer learning and fine-tuning phases. We identify three distinct mechanisms of AUC-consistency dissociation, invisible to standard classification metrics: threshold-mediated gold list collapse, technique-specific attribution collapse at peak AUC, and class-level consistency masking in global aggregation. C-Score provides an early warning signal of impending model instability. ScoreCAM deterioration on ResNet50V2 is detectable one full checkpoint before catastrophic AUC collapse and yields architecture-specific clinical deployment recommendations grounded in explanation quality rather than predictive ranking alone.

摘要：類別激活映射（CAM）方法被廣泛用於生成醫學影像中深度學習分類器的視覺解釋。<lb/>然而，現有的評估框架評估解釋是否正確，通過與放射科醫生註釋的定位忠實度來衡量，而不是評估它們是否一致：即模型是否在具有相同病理的不同患者之間應用相同的空間推理策略。<lb/>我們提出了C-Score（一致性分數），這是一種基於信心加權的無註釋指標，通過強調強度的成對軟IoU量化類內解釋的可重複性，針對正確分類的實例。<lb/>我們在Kermany胸部X光數據集上評估六種CAM技術：GradCAM、GradCAM++、LayerCAM、EigenCAM、ScoreCAM和MS GradCAM++，涵蓋三種CNN架構（DenseNet201、InceptionV3、ResNet50V2），並在三十個訓練週期內進行轉移學習和微調階段的評估。<lb/>我們識別出三種AUC一致性解離的不同機制，這些機制對標準分類指標來說是不可見的：閾值介導的金名單崩潰、在峰值AUC時的技術特定歸因崩潰，以及在全局聚合中的類別級一致性掩蔽。<lb/>C-Score提供了即將發生的模型不穩定性的早期警告信號。<lb/>在ResNet50V2上，ScoreCAM的惡化在災難性AUC崩潰之前可以檢測到一個完整的檢查點，並基於解釋質量而非僅僅是預測排名，提供架構特定的臨床部署建議。

##### **A Machine Learning Framework for Turbofan Health Estimation via Inverse Problem Formulation**
2604.08460v1 by Milad Leyli-Abadi, Lucas Thil, Sebastien Razakarivony, Guillaume Doquet, Jesse Read

Estimating the health state of turbofan engines is a challenging ill-posed inverse problem, hindered by sparse sensing and complex nonlinear thermodynamics. Research in this area remains fragmented, with comparisons limited by the use of unrealistic datasets and insufficient exploration of the exploitation of temporal information. This work investigates how to recover component-level health indicators from operational sensor data under realistic degradation and maintenance patterns. To support this study, we introduce a new dataset that incorporates industry-oriented complexities such as maintenance events and usage changes. Using this dataset, we establish an initial benchmark that compares steady-state and nonstationary data-driven models, and Bayesian filters, classic families of methods used to solve this problem. In addition to this benchmark, we introduce self-supervised learning (SSL) approaches that learn latent representations without access to true health labels, a scenario reflective of real-world operational constraints. By comparing the downstream estimation performance of these unsupervised representations against the direct prediction baselines, we establish a practical lower bound on the difficulty of solving this inverse problem. Our results reveal that traditional filters remain strong baselines, while SSL methods reveal the intrinsic complexity of health estimation and highlight the need for more advanced and interpretable inference strategies. For reproducibility, both the generated dataset and the implementation used in this work are made accessible.

摘要：估計渦扇發動機的健康狀態是一個具有挑戰性的病態反問題，受到稀疏感測和複雜非線性熱力學的阻礙。這個領域的研究仍然是支離破碎的，因為比較受到不現實數據集的限制，以及對時間信息利用的探索不足。這項工作研究如何在現實的退化和維護模式下，從操作傳感器數據中恢復組件級健康指標。為了支持這項研究，我們引入了一個新的數據集，該數據集考慮了行業導向的複雜性，例如維護事件和使用變化。利用這個數據集，我們建立了一個初步基準，對比穩態和非穩態數據驅動模型，以及貝葉斯濾波器，這些都是用來解決這個問題的經典方法家族。除了這個基準，我們還引入了自我監督學習（SSL）方法，這些方法在沒有真實健康標籤的情況下學習潛在表示，這是一種反映現實操作約束的情境。通過將這些無監督表示的下游估計性能與直接預測基準進行比較，我們確立了解決這個反問題的難度的實際下限。我們的結果顯示，傳統濾波器仍然是強有力的基準，而SSL方法揭示了健康估計的內在複雜性，並強調了對更先進和可解釋的推斷策略的需求。為了可重複性，這項工作中生成的數據集和實施方法都已公開。

##### **Lost in the Hype: Revealing and Dissecting the Performance Degradation of Medical Multimodal Large Language Models in Image Classification**
2604.08333v1 by Xun Zhu, Fanbin Mo, Xi Chen, Kaili Zheng, Shaoshuai Yang, Yiming Shi, Jian Gao, Miao Li, Ji Wu

The rise of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) has sparked an unprecedented wave of applications in the field of medical imaging analysis. However, as one of the earliest and most fundamental tasks integrated into this paradigm, medical image classification reveals a sobering reality: state-of-the-art medical MLLMs consistently underperform compared to traditional deep learning models, despite their overwhelming advantages in pre-training data and model parameters. This paradox prompts a critical rethinking: where exactly does the performance degradation originate? In this paper, we conduct extensive experiments on 14 open-source medical MLLMs across three representative image classification datasets. Moving beyond superficial performance benchmarking, we employ feature probing to track the information flow of visual features module-by-module and layer-by-layer throughout the entire MLLM pipeline, enabling explicit visualization of where and how classification signals are distorted, diluted, or overridden. As the first attempt to dissect classification performance degradation in medical MLLMs, our findings reveal four failure modes: 1) quality limitation in visual representation, 2) fidelity loss in connector projection, 3) comprehension deficit in LLM reasoning, and 4) misalignment of semantic mapping. Meanwhile, we introduce quantitative scores that characterize the healthiness of feature evolution, enabling principled comparisons across diverse MLLMs and datasets. Furthermore, we provide insightful discussions centered on the critical barriers that prevent current medical MLLMs from fulfilling their promised clinical potential. We hope that our work provokes rethinking within the community-highlighting that the road from high expectations to clinically deployable MLLMs remains long and winding.

摘要：多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）的興起在醫學影像分析領域引發了前所未有的應用浪潮。<lb/>然而，作為這一範式中最早且最基本的任務之一，醫學影像分類揭示了一個令人清醒的現實：儘管在預訓練數據和模型參數上具有壓倒性的優勢，最先進的醫學MLLMs在性能上仍然不及傳統深度學習模型。<lb/>這一悖論促使我們進行重要的重新思考：性能下降究竟源於何處？<lb/>在本文中，我們對14個開源醫學MLLMs在三個具有代表性的影像分類數據集上進行了廣泛的實驗。<lb/>超越表面的性能基準，我們採用特徵探測方法，逐模塊和逐層追蹤視覺特徵的信息流，從而明確可視化分類信號在何處以及如何被扭曲、稀釋或覆蓋。<lb/>作為首次試圖剖析醫學MLLMs中分類性能下降的研究，我們的發現揭示了四種失敗模式：1）視覺表徵的質量限制，2）連接器投影中的保真度損失，3）LLM推理中的理解缺陷，以及4）語義映射的不對齊。<lb/>同時，我們引入了量化分數來表徵特徵演變的健康性，從而實現不同MLLMs和數據集之間的原則性比較。<lb/>此外，我們提供了有見地的討論，集中於當前醫學MLLMs無法實現其承諾的臨床潛力的關鍵障礙。<lb/>我們希望我們的工作能夠引發社群的重新思考，強調從高期望到可臨床部署的MLLMs之路仍然漫長而曲折。

##### **ProMedical: Hierarchical Fine-Grained Criteria Modeling for Medical LLM Alignment via Explicit Injection**
2604.08326v1 by He Geng, Yangmin Huang, Lixian Lai, Qianyun Du, Hui Chu, Zhiyang He, Jiaxue Hu, Xiaodong Tao

Aligning Large Language Models (LLMs) with high-stakes medical standards remains a significant challenge, primarily due to the dissonance between coarse-grained preference signals and the complex, multi-dimensional nature of clinical protocols. To bridge this gap, we introduce ProMedical, a unified alignment framework grounded in fine-grained clinical criteria. We first construct ProMedical-Preference-50k, a dataset generated via a human-in-the-loop pipeline that augments medical instructions with rigorous, physician-derived rubrics. Leveraging this corpus, we propose the Explicit Criteria Injection paradigm to train a multi-dimensional reward model. Unlike traditional scalar reward models, our approach explicitly disentangles safety constraints from general proficiency, enabling precise guidance during reinforcement learning. To rigorously validate this framework, we establish ProMedical-Bench, a held-out evaluation suite anchored by double-blind expert adjudication. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that optimizing the Qwen3-8B base model via ProMedical-RM-guided GRPO yields substantial gains, improving overall accuracy by 22.3% and safety compliance by 21.7%, effectively rivaling proprietary frontier models. Furthermore, the aligned policy generalizes robustly to external benchmarks, demonstrating performance comparable to state-of-the-art models on UltraMedical. We publicly release our datasets, reward models, and benchmarks to facilitate reproducible research in safety-aware medical alignment.

摘要：將大型語言模型（LLMs）與高風險醫療標準對齊仍然是一個重大挑戰，主要是由於粗略偏好信號與臨床協議的複雜多維性之間的矛盾。為了填補這一空白，我們介紹了ProMedical，一個基於細緻臨床標準的統一對齊框架。我們首先構建了ProMedical-Preference-50k，這是一個通過人機協作流程生成的數據集，該流程使用嚴格的醫生導出標準增強醫療指令。利用這個語料庫，我們提出了明確標準注入範式來訓練多維獎勵模型。與傳統的標量獎勵模型不同，我們的方法明確地將安全約束與一般能力分離，從而在強化學習過程中提供精確的指導。為了嚴格驗證這一框架，我們建立了ProMedical-Bench，一個由雙盲專家裁定支持的保留評估套件。實證評估表明，通過ProMedical-RM引導的GRPO優化Qwen3-8B基礎模型可實現顯著增益，整體準確性提高22.3%，安全合規性提高21.7%，有效地與專有前沿模型相抗衡。此外，對齊政策在外部基準上具有強大的泛化能力，顯示出在UltraMedical上與最先進模型相當的性能。我們公開發布了我們的數據集、獎勵模型和基準，以促進安全意識醫療對齊的可重複研究。

#### Abstracts
##### **Using Large Language Models and Knowledge Graphs to Improve the Interpretability of Machine Learning Models in Manufacturing**
2604.16280v1 by Thomas Bayer, Alexander Lohr, Sarah Weiß, Bernd Michelberger, Wolfram Höpken

Explaining Machine Learning (ML) results in a transparent and user-friendly manner remains a challenging task of Explainable Artificial Intelligence (XAI). In this paper, we present a method to enhance the interpretability of ML models by using a Knowledge Graph (KG). We store domain-specific data along with ML results and their corresponding explanations, establishing a structured connection between domain knowledge and ML insights. To make these insights accessible to users, we designed a selective retrieval method in which relevant triplets are extracted from the KG and processed by a Large Language Model (LLM) to generate user-friendly explanations of ML results. We evaluated our method in a manufacturing environment using the XAI Question Bank. Beyond standard questions, we introduce more complex, tailored questions that highlight the strengths of our approach. We evaluated 33 questions, analyzing responses using quantitative metrics such as accuracy and consistency, as well as qualitative ones such as clarity and usefulness. Our contribution is both theoretical and practical: from a theoretical perspective, we present a novel approach for effectively enabling LLMs to dynamically access a KG in order to improve the explainability of ML results. From a practical perspective, we provide empirical evidence showing that such explanations can be successfully applied in real-world manufacturing environments, supporting better decision-making in manufacturing processes.

摘要：解釋機器學習（ML）結果以透明且使用者友好的方式仍然是可解釋人工智慧（XAI）的一項挑戰性任務。在本文中，我們提出了一種通過使用知識圖譜（KG）來增強ML模型可解釋性的方法。我們儲存領域特定的數據以及ML結果及其相應的解釋，建立領域知識與ML見解之間的結構化連結。為了使這些見解對使用者可訪問，我們設計了一種選擇性檢索方法，從KG中提取相關的三元組，並由大型語言模型（LLM）處理，以生成使用者友好的ML結果解釋。我們在製造環境中使用XAI問題庫評估我們的方法。除了標準問題外，我們還引入了更複雜、量身定制的問題，以突顯我們方法的優勢。我們評估了33個問題，使用準確性和一致性等定量指標，以及清晰度和有用性等定性指標來分析回應。我們的貢獻既具有理論性也具有實踐性：從理論的角度來看，我們提出了一種新穎的方法，能夠有效地使LLM動態訪問KG，以改善ML結果的可解釋性。從實踐的角度來看，我們提供了實證證據，顯示這樣的解釋可以成功應用於現實世界的製造環境中，支持更好的製造過程決策。

##### **BAGEL: Benchmarking Animal Knowledge Expertise in Language Models**
2604.16241v1 by Jiacheng Shen, Masato Hagiwara, Milad Alizadeh, Ellen Gilsenan-McMahon, Marius Miron, David Robinson, Emmanuel Chemla, Sara Keen, Gagan Narula, Mathieu Laurière, Matthieu Geist, Olivier Pietquin

Large language models have shown strong performance on broad-domain knowledge and reasoning benchmarks, but it remains unclear how well language models handle specialized animal-related knowledge under a unified closed-book evaluation protocol. We introduce BAGEL, a benchmark for evaluating animal knowledge expertise in language models. BAGEL is constructed from diverse scientific and reference sources, including bioRxiv, Global Biotic Interactions, Xeno-canto, and Wikipedia, using a combination of curated examples and automatically generated closed-book question-answer pairs. The benchmark covers multiple aspects of animal knowledge, including taxonomy, morphology, habitat, behavior, vocalization, geographic distribution, and species interactions. By focusing on closed-book evaluation, BAGEL measures animal-related knowledge of models without external retrieval at inference time. BAGEL further supports fine-grained analysis across source domains, taxonomic groups, and knowledge categories, enabling a more precise characterization of model strengths and systematic failure modes. Our benchmark provides a new testbed for studying domain-specific knowledge generalization in language models and for improving their reliability in biodiversity-related applications.

摘要：大型語言模型在廣泛領域的知識和推理基準上表現出色，但尚不清楚語言模型在統一的閉卷評估協議下如何處理專門的動物相關知識。我們介紹了BAGEL，一個用於評估語言模型中動物知識專業性的基準。BAGEL是從多種科學和參考來源構建的，包括bioRxiv、Global Biotic Interactions、Xeno-canto和維基百科，使用精心策劃的示例和自動生成的閉卷問答對的組合。該基準涵蓋了動物知識的多個方面，包括分類學、形態學、棲息地、行為、聲音、地理分佈和物種互動。通過專注於閉卷評估，BAGEL在推理時不依賴外部檢索來測量模型的動物相關知識。BAGEL還支持跨來源領域、分類群和知識類別的細緻分析，使模型的優勢和系統性失敗模式能夠更精確地表徵。我們的基準為研究語言模型中的領域特定知識泛化以及提高其在生物多樣性相關應用中的可靠性提供了一個新的測試平台。

##### **Neuro-Symbolic ODE Discovery with Latent Grammar Flow**
2604.16232v1 by Karin Yu, Eleni Chatzi, Georgios Kissas

Understanding natural and engineered systems often relies on symbolic formulations, such as differential equations, which provide interpretability and transferability beyond black-box models.
  We introduce Latent Grammar Flow (LGF), a neuro-symbolic generative framework for discovering ordinary differential equations from data. LGF embeds equations as grammar-based representations into a discrete latent space and forces semantically similar equations to be positioned closer together with a behavioural loss. Then, a discrete flow model guides the sampling process to recursively generate candidate equations that best fit the observed data. Domain knowledge and constraints, such as stability, can be either embedded into the rules or used as conditional predictors.

摘要：理解自然和工程系統通常依賴於符號化的公式，例如微分方程，這些公式提供了超越黑箱模型的可解釋性和可轉移性。<lb/>我們介紹潛在語法流（Latent Grammar Flow, LGF），這是一個神經符號生成框架，用於從數據中發現常微分方程。<lb/>LGF 將方程嵌入為基於語法的表示，進入離散潛在空間，並強迫語義上相似的方程彼此靠近，通過行為損失來實現。<lb/>然後，離散流模型引導採樣過程，遞歸生成最符合觀察數據的候選方程。<lb/>領域知識和約束條件，例如穩定性，可以嵌入到規則中或用作條件預測變數。

##### **Training Time Prediction for Mixed Precision-based Distributed Training**
2604.16145v1 by Minchul Kang, Changyong Shin, Jinwoo Jeong, Hyunho Lee, Younghun Go, Gyeongmin Kim, Gyeongsik Yang, Chuck Yoo

Accurate prediction of training time in distributed deep learning is crucial for resource allocation, cost estimation, and job scheduling. We observe that the floating-point precision setting is a key determinant of training time, leading to training time variations of ~2.4x over its minimum. However, existing studies on distributed training time prediction rely on static model computation graphs that do not capture precision variations, including mixed precision. According to our experiments, training time prediction without considering precision results in significant prediction errors - reaching up to 147.85% in mean absolute percentage error (MAPE). To address this issue, we propose a precision-aware distributed training time predictor that achieves robust accuracy across diverse precision settings, including mixed precision, with 9.8% MAPE.

摘要：準確預測分散式深度學習的訓練時間對資源分配、成本估算和工作排程至關重要。<lb/>我們觀察到浮點精度設置是訓練時間的關鍵決定因素，導致訓練時間的變化約為其最小值的2.4倍。<lb/>然而，現有的分散式訓練時間預測研究依賴於靜態模型計算圖，這些圖無法捕捉精度變化，包括混合精度。<lb/>根據我們的實驗，未考慮精度的訓練時間預測會導致顯著的預測誤差——平均絕對百分比誤差（MAPE）高達147.85%。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們提出了一種精度感知的分散式訓練時間預測器，能在多種精度設置下，包括混合精度，實現穩健的準確性，MAPE為9.8%。

##### **AgentV-RL: Scaling Reward Modeling with Agentic Verifier**
2604.16004v1 by Jiazheng Zhang, Ziche Fu, Zhiheng Xi, Wenqing Jing, Mingxu Chai, Wei He, Guoqiang Zhang, Chenghao Fan, Chenxin An, Wenxiang Chen, Zhicheng Liu, Haojie Pan, Dingwei Zhu, Tao Gui, Qi Zhang, Xuanjing Huang

Verifiers have been demonstrated to enhance LLM reasoning via test-time scaling (TTS). Yet, they face significant challenges in complex domains. Error propagation from incorrect intermediate reasoning can lead to false positives for seemingly plausible solutions, while lacking external grounding makes verifiers unreliable on computation or knowledge-intensive tasks. To address these challenges, we propose Agentic Verifier, a framework that transforms reward modeling into a multi-turn, tool-augmented deliberative process. We introduce complementary forward and backward agents: one traces solutions from premises to conclusions, while the other re-checks conclusions against their underlying premises. This bidirectional process enables a comprehensive, reliable, and interpretable assessment of solutions. To facilitate practical deployment, we propose AgentV-RL. Through proactive exploration and reinforcement learning, the verifier autonomously interleaves tool-use with internal reasoning. Extensive experiments show that Agentic Verifier yields consistent performance gains under both parallel and sequential TTS. Notably, our 4B variant surpasses state-of-the-art ORMs by 25.2%, positioning it as a promising paradigm for agentic reward modeling.

摘要：驗證器已被證明能通過測試時擴展（TTS）增強大型語言模型（LLM）的推理能力。<lb/>然而，它們在複雜領域面臨重大挑戰。<lb/>來自不正確中間推理的錯誤傳播可能導致看似合理解決方案的假陽性，而缺乏外部基礎使得驗證器在計算或知識密集型任務上變得不可靠。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了Agentic Verifier，一個將獎勵建模轉化為多回合、工具增強的深思過程的框架。<lb/>我們引入了互補的前向和後向代理：一個從前提追溯到結論，另一個則將結論與其基礎前提進行重新檢查。<lb/>這一雙向過程使得對解決方案的評估變得全面、可靠且可解釋。<lb/>為了促進實際部署，我們提出了AgentV-RL。<lb/>通過主動探索和強化學習，驗證器自主地將工具使用與內部推理交織在一起。<lb/>大量實驗表明，Agentic Verifier在平行和序列TTS下均能持續提升性能。<lb/>值得注意的是，我們的4B變體超越了最先進的ORM，提升幅度達25.2%，使其成為一種有前景的代理獎勵建模範式。

##### **SCHK-HTC: Sibling Contrastive Learning with Hierarchical Knowledge-Aware Prompt Tuning for Hierarchical Text Classification**
2604.15998v1 by Ke Xiong, Qian Wu, Wangjie Gan, Yuke Li, Xuhong Zhang

Few-shot Hierarchical Text Classification (few-shot HTC) is a challenging task that involves mapping texts to a predefined tree-structured label hierarchy under data-scarce conditions. While current approaches utilize structural constraints from the label hierarchy to maintain parent-child prediction consistency, they face a critical bottleneck, the difficulty in distinguishing semantically similar sibling classes due to insufficient domain knowledge. We introduce an innovative method named Sibling Contrastive Learning with Hierarchical Knowledge-aware Prompt Tuning for few-shot HTC tasks (SCHK-HTC). Our work enhances the model's perception of subtle differences between sibling classes at deeper levels, rather than just enforcing hierarchical rules. Specifically, we propose a novel framework featuring two core components: a hierarchical knowledge extraction module and a sibling contrastive learning mechanism. This design guides model to encode discriminative features at each hierarchy level, thus improving the separability of confusable classes. Our approach achieves superior performance across three benchmark datasets, surpassing existing state-of-the-art methods in most cases. Our code is available at https://github.com/happywinder/SCHK-HTC.

摘要：少樣本層級文本分類（few-shot HTC）是一項具有挑戰性的任務，涉及在數據稀缺的條件下將文本映射到預定的樹狀標籤層級結構中。雖然當前的方法利用標籤層級的結構約束來保持父子預測的一致性，但它們面臨一個關鍵瓶頸，即由於領域知識不足，難以區分語義上相似的兄弟類別。我們提出了一種創新的方法，名為具有層級知識感知提示調整的兄弟對比學習，用於少樣本 HTC 任務（SCHK-HTC）。我們的工作增強了模型對兄弟類別之間細微差異的感知，而不僅僅是強制執行層級規則。具體而言，我們提出了一個新穎的框架，具有兩個核心組件：一個層級知識提取模塊和一個兄弟對比學習機制。這一設計指導模型在每個層級編碼區分特徵，從而提高可混淆類別的可分性。我們的方法在三個基準數據集上達到了優越的性能，在大多數情況下超越了現有的最先進方法。我們的代碼可在 https://github.com/happywinder/SCHK-HTC 獲得。

##### **ReactBench: A Benchmark for Topological Reasoning in MLLMs on Chemical Reaction Diagrams**
2604.15994v1 by Qiang Xu, Shengyuan Bai, Yu Wang, He Cao, Leqing Chen, Yuanyuan Liu, Bin Feng, Zijing Liu, Yu Li

Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) excel at recognizing individual visual elements and reasoning over simple linear diagrams. However, when faced with complex topological structures involving branching paths, converging flows, and cyclic dependencies, their reasoning capabilities degrade sharply, even on tasks as basic as counting endpoints. Existing benchmarks fail to probe this gap, focusing on semantic comprehension rather than structural reasoning. We introduce ReactBench, a benchmark that reveals fundamental limitations in structural reasoning through chemical reaction diagrams. These real-world scientific diagrams offer an ideal testbed because they naturally span diverse structures from linear chains to cyclic graphs, while requiring both precise local recognition and coherent global reasoning. Our benchmark comprises 1,618 expert-annotated QA pairs across four hierarchical task dimensions. Extensive evaluation across 17 MLLMs reveals a significant performance gap exceeding 30% between anchor-based tasks and holistic structural reasoning tasks. Controlled ablations confirm this bottleneck lies in reasoning, not perception. These findings expose a fundamental deficit in structural understanding and establish directions for advancing visual reasoning.

摘要：多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）在識別個別視覺元素和推理簡單線性圖表方面表現出色。<lb/>然而，當面對涉及分支路徑、匯聚流和循環依賴的複雜拓撲結構時，它們的推理能力急劇下降，即使在計算端點這樣基本的任務上也是如此。<lb/>現有的基準無法探測這一差距，專注於語義理解而非結構推理。<lb/>我們介紹了ReactBench，這是一個通過化學反應圖揭示結構推理基本限制的基準。<lb/>這些現實世界的科學圖表提供了理想的測試平台，因為它們自然涵蓋了從線性鏈到循環圖的多樣結構，同時需要精確的局部識別和連貫的全局推理。<lb/>我們的基準由1,618對專家註釋的問答對組成，涵蓋四個層次的任務維度。<lb/>在17個MLLMs上進行的廣泛評估顯示，基於錨點的任務與整體結構推理任務之間存在超過30%的顯著性能差距。<lb/>控制性消融實驗確認這一瓶頸存在於推理，而非感知。<lb/>這些發現揭示了結構理解的基本不足，並為推進視覺推理建立了方向。

##### **Integrating Graphs, Large Language Models, and Agents: Reasoning and Retrieval**
2604.15951v1 by Hamed Jelodar, Samita Bai, Mohammad Meymani, Parisa Hamedi, Roozbeh Razavi-Far, Ali Ghorbani

Generative AI, particularly Large Language Models, increasingly integrates graph-based representations to enhance reasoning, retrieval, and structured decision-making. Despite rapid advances, there remains limited clarity regarding when, why, where, and what types of graph-LLM integrations are most appropriate across applications. This survey provides a concise, structured overview of the design choices underlying the integration of graphs with LLMs. We categorize existing methods based on their purpose (reasoning, retrieval, generation, recommendation), graph modality (knowledge graphs, scene graphs, interaction graphs, causal graphs, dependency graphs), and integration strategies (prompting, augmentation, training, or agent-based use). ##### **RAGognizer: Hallucination-Aware Fine-Tuning via Detection Head Integration**
2604.15945v1 by Fabian Ridder, Laurin Lessel, Malte Schilling

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) is widely used to augment the input to Large Language Models (LLMs) with external information, such as recent or domain-specific knowledge. Nonetheless, current models still produce closed-domain hallucinations and generate content that is unsupported by the retrieved context. Current detection approaches typically treat hallucination as a post-hoc problem, relying on black-box consistency checks or probes over frozen internal representations. In this work, we demonstrate that hallucination detection based on internal state representation can also serve as a direct training signal. We introduce RAGognize, a dataset of naturally occurring closed-domain hallucinations with token-level annotations, and RAGognizer, a hallucination-aware fine-tuning approach that integrates a lightweight detection head into an LLM, allowing for the joint optimization of language modeling and hallucination detection. This joint objective forces the model to improve the separability of its internal states regarding hallucinations while simultaneously learning to generate well-formed and meaningful responses. Across multiple benchmarks, RAGognizer achieves state-of-the-art token-level hallucination detection while substantially reducing hallucination rates during generation, without degrading language quality or relevance.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）被廣泛用於通過外部信息來增強大型語言模型（LLMs）的輸入，例如最近的或特定領域的知識。<lb/>然而，當前的模型仍然會產生封閉領域的幻覺，並生成不受檢索上下文支持的內容。<lb/>目前的檢測方法通常將幻覺視為事後問題，依賴於黑箱一致性檢查或對凍結的內部表示進行探測。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們展示了基於內部狀態表示的幻覺檢測也可以作為直接的訓練信號。<lb/>我們引入了RAGognize，一個自然發生的封閉領域幻覺數據集，並附有標記級別的註釋，以及RAGognizer，一種幻覺感知的微調方法，將輕量級檢測頭集成到LLM中，允許語言建模和幻覺檢測的聯合優化。<lb/>這一聯合目標迫使模型改善其內部狀態在幻覺方面的可分性，同時學習生成結構良好且有意義的回應。<lb/>在多個基準測試中，RAGognizer實現了最先進的標記級幻覺檢測，同時在生成過程中顯著降低了幻覺率，且不降低語言質量或相關性。

##### **Experience Compression Spectrum: Unifying Memory, Skills, and Rules in LLM Agents**
2604.15877v1 by Xing Zhang, Guanghui Wang, Yanwei Cui, Wei Qiu, Ziyuan Li, Bing Zhu, Peiyang He

As LLM agents scale to long-horizon, multi-session deployments, efficiently managing accumulated experience becomes a critical bottleneck. Agent memory systems and agent skill discovery both address this challenge -- extracting reusable knowledge from interaction traces -- yet a citation analysis of 1,136 references across 22 primary papers reveals a cross-community citation rate below 1%. We propose the \emph{Experience Compression Spectrum}, a unifying framework that positions memory, skills, and rules as points along a single axis of increasing compression (5--20$\times$ for episodic memory, 50--500$\times$ for procedural skills, 1,000$\times$+ for declarative rules), directly reducing context consumption, retrieval latency, and compute overhead. Mapping 20+ systems onto this spectrum reveals that every system operates at a fixed, predetermined compression level -- none supports adaptive cross-level compression, a gap we term the \emph{missing diagonal}. We further show that specialization alone is insufficient -- both communities independently solve shared sub-problems without exchanging solutions -- that evaluation methods are tightly coupled to compression levels, that transferability increases with compression at the cost of specificity, and that knowledge lifecycle management remains largely neglected. We articulate open problems and design principles for scalable, full-spectrum agent learning systems.

摘要：隨著 LLM 代理在長期、多會話的部署中擴展，有效管理累積的經驗成為一個關鍵瓶頸。代理記憶系統和代理技能發現都針對這一挑戰——從互動痕跡中提取可重用的知識——然而對 22 篇主要論文中 1,136 篇參考文獻的引用分析顯示，跨社群的引用率低於 1%。我們提出了 \emph{經驗壓縮光譜}，這是一個統一框架，將記憶、技能和規則定位於一個隨著壓縮程度增加的單一軸線上（對於情節記憶為 5--20$\times$，對於程序技能為 50--500$\times$，對於陳述性規則為 1,000$\times$ 以上），直接減少上下文消耗、檢索延遲和計算開銷。將 20 多個系統映射到這個光譜上顯示，每個系統都在固定的、預定的壓縮水平上運作——沒有一個支持自適應的跨級壓縮，我們稱這一空白為 \emph{缺失的對角線}。我們進一步表明，單靠專業化是不夠的——兩個社群獨立解決共享的子問題而不交換解決方案——評估方法與壓縮水平緊密相關，轉移性隨著壓縮而增加，但特異性則降低，並且知識生命周期管理仍然在很大程度上被忽視。我們闡明了可擴展的全光譜代理學習系統的開放問題和設計原則。

##### **How Hypocritical Is Your LLM judge? Listener-Speaker Asymmetries in the Pragmatic Competence of Large Language Models**
2604.15873v1 by Judith Sieker, Sina Zarrieß

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly studied as repositories of linguistic knowledge. In this line of work, models are commonly evaluated both as generators of language and as judges of linguistic output, yet these two roles are rarely examined in direct relation to one another. As a result, it remains unclear whether success in one role aligns with success in the other. In this paper, we address this question for pragmatic competence by comparing LLMs' performance as pragmatic listeners, judging the appropriateness of linguistic outputs, and as pragmatic speakers, generating pragmatically appropriate language. We evaluate multiple open-weight and proprietary LLMs across three pragmatic settings. We find a robust asymmetry between pragmatic evaluation and pragmatic generation: many models perform substantially better as listeners than as speakers. Our results suggest that pragmatic judging and pragmatic generation are only weakly aligned in current LLMs, calling for more integrated evaluation practices.

##### **CiPO: Counterfactual Unlearning for Large Reasoning Models through Iterative Preference Optimization**
2604.15847v1 by Junyi Li, Yongqiang Chen, Ningning Ding

Machine unlearning has gained increasing attention in recent years, as a promising technique to selectively remove unwanted privacy or copyrighted information from Large Language Models that are trained on a massive scale of human data. However, the emergence of Large Reasoning Models (LRMs), which emphasize long chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning to address complex questions, presents a dilemma to unlearning: existing methods either struggle to completely eliminate undesired knowledge from the CoT traces or degrade the reasoning performances due to the interference with the reasoning process. To this end, we introduce Counterfactual Unlearning through iterative Preference Optimization (CiPO), a novel framework that redefines unlearning as the targeted intervention of the CoT reasoning in LRMs. More specifically, given a desired unlearning target answer, CiPO instructs LRMs to generate a logically valid counterfactual reasoning trace for preference tuning. As the LRM adjusts to the counterfactual trace, CiPO iteratively updates the preference learning data to increase the discrepancy from the original model. This iterative loop ensures both desirable unlearning and smooth optimization, effectively mitigating the dilemma. Experiments on challenging benchmarks demonstrate that CiPO excels at unlearning, completely removing knowledge from both the intermediate CoT steps and the final answer, while preserving the reasoning abilities of LRMs.

摘要：機器去學習在近年來受到越來越多的關注，作為一種有前景的技術，旨在從在大量人類數據上訓練的大型語言模型中選擇性地移除不需要的隱私或版權信息。<lb/>然而，大型推理模型（LRMs）的出現，強調長鏈思考（CoT）推理以解決複雜問題，為去學習帶來了困境：現有方法要麼難以徹底消除CoT痕跡中的不必要知識，要麼因為對推理過程的干擾而降低推理性能。<lb/>為此，我們介紹了通過迭代偏好優化的反事實去學習（CiPO），這是一個新穎的框架，將去學習重新定義為對LRMs中CoT推理的有針對性的干預。<lb/>更具體地說，給定一個期望的去學習目標答案，CiPO指導LRMs生成一個邏輯上有效的反事實推理痕跡以進行偏好調整。<lb/>隨著LRM適應反事實痕跡，CiPO迭代更新偏好學習數據，以增加與原始模型的差異。<lb/>這個迭代循環確保了既期望的去學習又平滑的優化，有效地緩解了困境。<lb/>在挑戰性基準上的實驗表明，CiPO在去學習方面表現出色，徹底移除了中間CoT步驟和最終答案中的知識，同時保留了LRMs的推理能力。

##### **CHOP: Chunkwise Context-Preserving Framework for RAG on Multi Documents**
2604.15802v1 by Hyunseok Park, Jihyeon Kim, Jongeun Kim, Dongsik Yoon

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems lose retrieval accuracy when similar documents coexist in the vector database, causing unnecessary information, hallucinations, and factual errors. To alleviate this issue, we propose CHOP, a framework that iteratively evaluates chunk relevance with Large Language Models (LLMs) and progressively reconstructs documents by determining their association with specific topics or query types. CHOP integrates two key components: the CNM-Extractor, which generates compact per-chunk signatures capturing categories, key nouns, and model names, and the Continuity Decision Module, which preserves contextual coherence by deciding whether consecutive chunks belong to the same document flow. By prefixing each chunk with context-aware metadata, CHOP reduces semantic conflicts among similar documents and enhances retriever discrimination. Experiments on benchmark datasets show that CHOP alleviates retrieval confusion and provides a scalable approach for building high-quality knowledge bases, achieving a Top-1 Hit Rate of 90.77% and notable gains in ranking quality metrics.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）系統在向量數據庫中存在相似文檔時會失去檢索準確性，導致不必要的信息、幻覺和事實錯誤。為了緩解這一問題，我們提出了CHOP，一個通過大型語言模型（LLMs）迭代評估塊相關性的框架，並通過確定其與特定主題或查詢類型的關聯來逐步重建文檔。CHOP整合了兩個關鍵組件：CNM-Extractor，該組件生成緊湊的每個塊簽名，以捕捉類別、關鍵名詞和模型名稱，以及連續性決策模塊，該模塊通過決定連續塊是否屬於同一文檔流來保持上下文的一致性。通過在每個塊前加上上下文感知的元數據，CHOP減少了相似文檔之間的語義衝突，並增強了檢索器的區分能力。在基準數據集上的實驗表明，CHOP緩解了檢索混淆，並提供了一種可擴展的方法來構建高質量的知識庫，實現了90.77%的Top-1命中率和在排名質量指標上顯著的增益。

##### **EVIL: Evolving Interpretable Algorithms for Zero-Shot Inference on Event Sequences and Time Series with LLMs**
2604.15787v1 by David Berghaus

We introduce EVIL (\textbf{EV}olving \textbf{I}nterpretable algorithms with \textbf{L}LMs), an approach that uses LLM-guided evolutionary search to discover simple, interpretable algorithms for dynamical systems inference. Rather than training neural networks on large datasets, EVIL evolves pure Python/NumPy programs that perform zero-shot, in-context inference across datasets. We apply EVIL to three distinct tasks: next-event prediction in temporal point processes, rate matrix estimation for Markov jump processes, and time series imputation. In each case, a single evolved algorithm generalizes across all evaluation datasets without per-dataset training (analogous to an amortized inference model). To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to show that LLM-guided program evolution can discover a single compact inference function for these dynamical-systems problems. Across the three domains, the discovered algorithms are often competitive with, and even outperform, state-of-the-art deep learning models while being orders of magnitudes faster, and remaining fully interpretable.

摘要：我們介紹了 EVIL (\textbf{EV}olving \textbf{I}nterpretable algorithms with \textbf{L}LMs)，這是一種利用 LLM 指導的進化搜索來發現簡單、可解釋的動態系統推斷算法的方法。與其在大型數據集上訓練神經網絡，EVIL 演化出純 Python/NumPy 程式，能夠在數據集之間進行零樣本、上下文推斷。我們將 EVIL 應用於三個不同的任務：時間點過程中的下一事件預測、馬爾可夫跳躍過程的速率矩陣估計，以及時間序列插補。在每種情況下，單一演化的算法能夠在所有評估數據集上進行泛化，而無需針對每個數據集進行訓練（類似於攤銷推斷模型）。據我們所知，這是首個顯示 LLM 指導的程式演化能夠為這些動態系統問題發現單一緊湊推斷函數的研究。在這三個領域中，所發現的算法通常與最先進的深度學習模型競爭，甚至超越它們，同時速度快上數個量級，並保持完全可解釋性。

##### **Phase Transitions as the Breakdown of Statistical Indistinguishability**
2604.15773v1 by Taiyo Narita, Hideyuki Miyahara

We introduce a novel characterization of phase transitions based on hypothesis testing.
  In our formulation, a phase transition is defined as the breakdown of statistical indistinguishability under vanishing parameter perturbations in the thermodynamic limit.
  This perspective provides a general, order-parameter-free framework that does not rely on model-specific insights or learning procedures.
  We show that conventional approaches, such as those based on the Binder parameter, can be reinterpreted as special cases within this framework.
  As a concrete realization, we employ a distribution-free two-sample run test and demonstrate that the critical point of the two-dimensional Ising model is accurately identified without prior knowledge of the order parameter.
