##### **Co-FactChecker: A Framework for Human-AI Collaborative Claim Verification Using Large Reasoning Models**
2604.13706v1 by Dhruv Sahnan, Subhabrata Dutta, Tanmoy Chakraborty, Preslav Nakov, Iryna Gurevych

Professional fact-checkers rely on domain knowledge and deep contextual understanding to verify claims. Large language models (LLMs) and large reasoning models (LRMs) lack such grounding and primarily reason from available evidence alone, creating a mismatch between expert-led and fully automated claim verification. To mitigate this gap, we posit human-AI collaboration as a more promising path forward, where expert feedback, grounded in real-world knowledge and domain expertise, guides the model's reasoning. However, existing LRMs are hard to calibrate to natural language feedback, particularly in a multi-turn interaction setup. We propose Co-FactChecker, a framework for human-AI collaborative claim verification. We introduce a new interaction paradigm that treats the model's thinking trace as a shared scratchpad. Co-FactChecker translates expert feedback into trace-edits that introduce targeted modifications to the trace, sidestepping the shortcomings of dialogue-based interaction. We provide theoretical results showing that trace-editing offers advantages over multi-turn dialogue, and our automatic evaluations demonstrate that Co-FactChecker outperforms existing autonomous and human-AI collaboration approaches. Human evaluations further show that Co-FactChecker is preferred over multi-turn dialogue, producing higher quality reasoning and verdicts along with relatively easier to interpret and more useful thinking traces.

摘要：專業事實查核者依賴領域知識和深厚的背景理解來驗證主張。大型語言模型（LLMs）和大型推理模型（LRMs）缺乏這種基礎，主要僅依賴可用的證據進行推理，造成專家主導的驗證與完全自動化的主張驗證之間的不匹配。為了減少這個差距，我們提出人類與人工智慧的合作作為更有前景的前進方向，在這種合作中，基於現實世界知識和領域專業的專家反饋指導模型的推理。然而，現有的LRMs很難調整以適應自然語言反饋，特別是在多輪互動的設置中。我們提出Co-FactChecker，一個人類與人工智慧合作的主張驗證框架。我們引入一種新的互動範式，將模型的思維痕跡視為共享的草稿板。Co-FactChecker將專家反饋轉換為痕跡編輯，對痕跡進行針對性的修改，避開基於對話互動的缺陷。我們提供理論結果顯示，痕跡編輯相比多輪對話具有優勢，我們的自動評估顯示Co-FactChecker優於現有的自主和人類-人工智慧合作方法。人類評估進一步顯示，Co-FactChecker比多輪對話更受偏好，產生更高質量的推理和裁決，並且其思維痕跡相對更易於解釋且更有用。

##### **IndicDB -- Benchmarking Multilingual Text-to-SQL Capabilities in Indian Languages**
2604.13686v1 by Aviral Dawar, Roshan Karanth, Vikram Goyal, Dhruv Kumar

While Large Language Models (LLMs) have significantly advanced Text-to-SQL performance, existing benchmarks predominantly focus on Western contexts and simplified schemas, leaving a gap in real-world, non-Western applications. We present IndicDB, a multilingual Text-to-SQL benchmark for evaluating cross-lingual semantic parsing across diverse Indic languages. The relational schemas are sourced from open-data platforms, including the National Data and Analytics Platform (NDAP) and the India Data Portal (IDP), ensuring realistic administrative data complexity. IndicDB comprises 20 databases across 237 tables. To convert denormalized government data into rich relational structures, we employ an iterative three-agent framework (Architect, Auditor, Refiner) to ensure structural rigor and high relational density (11.85 tables per database; join depths up to six). Our pipeline is value-aware, difficulty-calibrated, and join-enforced, generating 15,617 tasks across English, Hindi, and five Indic languages. We evaluate cross-lingual semantic parsing performance of state-of-the-art models (DeepSeek v3.2, MiniMax 2.7, LLaMA 3.3, Qwen3) across seven linguistic variants. Results show a 9.00% performance drop from English to Indic languages, revealing an "Indic Gap" driven by harder schema linking, increased structural ambiguity, and limited external knowledge. IndicDB serves as a rigorous benchmark for multilingual Text-to-SQL. Code and data: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/multilingualText2Sql-Indic--DDCC/

摘要：雖然大型語言模型（LLMs）在文本到 SQL 的性能上有了顯著的進步，但現有的基準主要集中在西方背景和簡化的架構上，這在現實世界的非西方應用中留下了空白。我們提出了 IndicDB，這是一個多語言的文本到 SQL 基準，用於評估不同印度語言之間的跨語言語義解析。關係架構來自開放數據平台，包括國家數據與分析平台（NDAP）和印度數據門戶（IDP），確保了現實的行政數據複雜性。IndicDB 包含 20 個數據庫，涵蓋 237 個表。為了將非正規的政府數據轉換為豐富的關係結構，我們採用了迭代的三代理框架（架構師、審計師、精煉者），以確保結構的嚴謹性和高關係密度（每個數據庫 11.85 個表；連接深度最多達六）。我們的管道是價值感知的、難度校準的，並強制執行連接，生成了 15,617 個任務，涵蓋英語、印地語和五種印度語言。我們評估了最先進模型（DeepSeek v3.2、MiniMax 2.7、LLaMA 3.3、Qwen3）在七種語言變體中的跨語言語義解析性能。結果顯示，從英語到印度語言的性能下降了 9.00%，揭示了一個由於更難的架構連接、增加的結構模糊性和有限的外部知識所驅動的「印度差距」。IndicDB 作為多語言文本到 SQL 的嚴格基準。代碼和數據：https://anonymous.4open.science/r/multilingualText2Sql-Indic--DDCC/

##### **Automatically Inferring Teachers' Geometric Content Knowledge: A Skills Based Approach**
2604.13666v1 by Ziv Fenigstein, Kobi Gal, Avi Segal, Osama Swidan, Inbal Israel, Hassan Ayoob

Assessing teachers' geometric content knowledge is essential for geometry instructional quality and student learning, but difficult to scale. The Van Hiele model characterizes geometric reasoning through five hierarchical levels. Traditional Van Hiele assessment relies on manual expert analysis of open-ended responses. This process is time-consuming, costly, and prevents large-scale evaluation. This study develops an automated approach for diagnosing teachers' Van Hiele reasoning levels using large language models grounded in educational theory. Our central hypothesis is that integrating explicit skills information significantly improves Van Hiele classification. In collaboration with mathematics education researchers, we built a structured skills dictionary decomposing the Van Hiele levels into 33 fine-grained reasoning skills. Through a custom web platform, 31 pre-service teachers solved geometry problems, yielding 226 responses. Expert researchers then annotated each response with its Van Hiele level and demonstrated skills from the dictionary. Using this annotated dataset, we implemented two classification approaches: (1) retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) and (2) multi-task learning (MTL). Each approach compared a skills-aware variant incorporating the skills dictionary against a baseline without skills information. Results showed that for both methods, skills-aware variants significantly outperformed baselines across multiple evaluation metrics. This work provides the first automated approach for Van Hiele level classification from open-ended responses. It offers a scalable, theory-grounded method for assessing teachers' geometric reasoning that can enable large-scale evaluation and support adaptive, personalized teacher learning systems.

摘要：評估教師的幾何內容知識對於幾何教學質量和學生學習至關重要，但難以擴展。Van Hiele 模型通過五個層次來表徵幾何推理。傳統的 Van Hiele 評估依賴於對開放式回答的人工專家分析。這一過程耗時、成本高，並阻礙了大規模評估。本研究開發了一種自動化的方法，利用基於教育理論的大型語言模型來診斷教師的 Van Hiele 推理水平。我們的中心假設是，整合明確的技能信息顯著改善 Van Hiele 分類。與數學教育研究者合作，我們建立了一個結構化的技能詞典，將 Van Hiele 層次分解為 33 種細緻的推理技能。通過一個定制的網絡平台，31 名預備教師解決了幾何問題，產生了 226 個回答。專家研究人員隨後為每個回答標註了其 Van Hiele 層次和詞典中的顯示技能。利用這個標註數據集，我們實施了兩種分類方法：（1）檢索增強生成（RAG）和（2）多任務學習（MTL）。每種方法都比較了包含技能詞典的技能感知變體與不包含技能信息的基線。結果顯示，對於這兩種方法，技能感知變體在多個評估指標上顯著優於基線。這項工作提供了從開放式回答中自動化的 Van Hiele 層次分類的首個方法。它提供了一種可擴展的、基於理論的方法來評估教師的幾何推理，能夠支持大規模評估並促進適應性、個性化的教師學習系統。

##### **Debate to Align: Reliable Entity Alignment through Two-Stage Multi-Agent Debate**
2604.13551v1 by Cunda Wang, Ziying Ma, Po Hu, Weihua Wang, Feilong Bao

Entity alignment (EA) aims to identify entities referring to the same real-world object across different knowledge graphs (KGs). Recent approaches based on large language models (LLMs) typically obtain entity embeddings through knowledge representation learning and use embedding similarity to identify an alignment-uncertain entity set. For each uncertain entity, a candidate entity set (CES) is then retrieved based on embedding similarity to support subsequent alignment reasoning and decision making. However, the reliability of the CES and the reasoning capability of LLMs critically affect the effectiveness of subsequent alignment decisions. To address this issue, we propose AgentEA, a reliable EA framework based on multi-agent debate. AgentEA first improves embedding quality through entity representation preference optimization, and then introduces a two-stage multi-role debate mechanism consisting of lightweight debate verification and deep debate alignment to progressively enhance the reliability of alignment decisions while enabling more efficient debate-based reasoning. Extensive experiments on public benchmarks under cross-lingual, sparse, large-scale, and heterogeneous settings demonstrate the effectiveness of AgentEA.

摘要：實體對齊（EA）旨在識別不同知識圖譜（KGs）中指向相同現實世界對象的實體。最近基於大型語言模型（LLMs）的方法通常通過知識表示學習獲得實體嵌入，並使用嵌入相似度來識別對齊不確定的實體集。對於每個不確定的實體，然後根據嵌入相似度檢索候選實體集（CES），以支持後續的對齊推理和決策。然而，CES的可靠性和LLMs的推理能力對後續對齊決策的有效性有著至關重要的影響。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了AgentEA，一個基於多代理辯論的可靠EA框架。AgentEA首先通過實體表示偏好優化來提高嵌入質量，然後引入一個由輕量級辯論驗證和深度辯論對齊組成的兩階段多角色辯論機制，以逐步增強對齊決策的可靠性，同時實現更高效的基於辯論的推理。在跨語言、稀疏、大規模和異構設置下的公共基準上進行的大量實驗證明了AgentEA的有效性。

##### **Free Lunch for Unified Multimodal Models: Enhancing Generation via Reflective Rectification with Inherent Understanding**
2604.13540v1 by Yibo Jiang, Tao Wu, Rui Jiang, Yehao Lu, Chaoxiang Cai, Zequn Qin, Xi Li

Unified Multimodal Models (UMMs) aim to integrate visual understanding and generation within a single structure. However, these models exhibit a notable capability mismatch, where their understanding capability significantly outperforms their generation. This mismatch indicates that the model's rich internal knowledge, while effective for understanding tasks, remains underactivated during generation. To address this, we draw inspiration from the human ``Thinking-While-Drawing'' paradigm, where humans continuously reflect to activate their knowledge and rectify intermediate results. In this paper, we propose UniRect-CoT, a training-free unified rectification chain-of-thought framework. Our approach unlocks the ``free lunch'' hidden in the UMM's powerful inherent understanding to continuously reflect, activating its internal knowledge and rectifying intermediate results during generation.We regard the diffusion denoising process in UMMs as an intrinsic visual reasoning process and align the intermediate results with the target instruction understood by the model, serving as a self-supervisory signal to rectify UMM generation.Extensive experiments demonstrate that UniRect-CoT can be easily integrated into existing UMMs, significantly enhancing generation quality across diverse complex tasks.

摘要：統一多模態模型（UMMs）旨在將視覺理解和生成整合於單一結構中。<lb/>然而，這些模型顯示出顯著的能力不匹配，其中它們的理解能力遠超過其生成能力。<lb/>這種不匹配表明，模型豐富的內部知識在理解任務中雖然有效，但在生成過程中仍然未被充分激活。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們從人類的“邊畫邊思考”範式中獲得靈感，人類持續反思以激活他們的知識並修正中間結果。<lb/>在本文中，我們提出了UniRect-CoT，一個無需訓練的統一修正思維鏈框架。<lb/>我們的方法解鎖了UMM強大內在理解中隱藏的“免費午餐”，以持續反思，激活其內部知識並在生成過程中修正中間結果。<lb/>我們將UMMs中的擴散去噪過程視為一種內在的視覺推理過程，並將中間結果對齊模型理解的目標指令，作為自我監督信號來修正UMM生成。<lb/>大量實驗表明，UniRect-CoT可以輕鬆集成到現有的UMMs中，顯著提升各種複雜任務的生成質量。

##### **Synthesizing Instruction-Tuning Datasets with Contrastive Decoding**
2604.13538v1 by Tatsuya Ichinose, Youmi Ma, Masanari Oi, Ryuto Koike, Naoaki Okazaki

Using responses generated by high-performing large language models (LLMs) for instruction tuning has become a widely adopted approach. However, the existing literature overlooks a property of LLM-generated responses: they conflate world knowledge acquired during pre-training with instruction-following capabilities acquired during post-training. We hypothesize that disentangling the instruction-following capabilities from pre-trained knowledge improves the effectiveness of instruction tuning. To this end, we propose CoDIT, a method that applies contrastive decoding between a post-trained model and its pre-trained counterpart during response generation. The method suppresses pre-trained knowledge shared between the two models while amplifying the instruction-following behavior acquired via post-training, resulting in responses that more purely reflect instruction-following capabilities. Experiment results demonstrate that models trained on datasets constructed via CoDIT consistently outperform those trained on directly generated responses. Training on our datasets also yields better performance than on existing publicly available instruction-tuning datasets across multiple benchmarks. Furthermore, we theoretically and empirically show that CoDIT can be interpreted as distilling the chat vector from parameter space to text space, enabling the transfer of instruction-tuning capabilities across models of different architectures.

摘要：使用高效能大型語言模型（LLMs）生成的回應進行指令調整已成為一種廣泛採用的方法。<lb/>然而，現有文獻忽略了LLM生成回應的一個特性：它們將在預訓練期間獲得的世界知識與在後訓練期間獲得的遵循指令能力混為一談。<lb/>我們假設，將遵循指令的能力與預訓練知識分開，可以提高指令調整的有效性。<lb/>為此，我們提出了CoDIT，一種在回應生成過程中對後訓練模型和其預訓練對應模型進行對比解碼的方法。<lb/>該方法抑制了兩個模型之間共享的預訓練知識，同時增強了通過後訓練獲得的遵循指令行為，從而使回應更純粹地反映遵循指令的能力。<lb/>實驗結果顯示，基於CoDIT構建的數據集訓練的模型在性能上始終優於基於直接生成回應訓練的模型。<lb/>在我們的數據集上進行訓練的模型在多個基準測試中也比現有的公共可用指令調整數據集表現更佳。<lb/>此外，我們從理論和實證上表明，CoDIT可以被解釋為將聊天向量從參數空間提煉到文本空間，從而實現不同架構模型之間的指令調整能力轉移。

##### **Awakening Dormant Experts:Counterfactual Routing to Mitigate MoE Hallucinations**
2604.14246v1 by Wentao Hu, Yanbo Zhai, Xiaohui Hu, Mingkuan Zhao, Shanhong yu, Xue Liu, Kaidong Yu, Shuangyong Song, Xuelong Li

Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models have achieved remarkable scalability, yet they remain vulnerable to hallucinations, particularly when processing long-tail knowledge. We identify that this fragility stems from static Top-$k$ routing: routers tend to favor high-frequency patterns over rare factual associations. Consequently, ``specialist experts'' possessing critical long-tail knowledge are often assigned low gating scores and remain ``dormant'' -- under-prioritized for specific tokens despite their proven causal importance on other inputs. To address this, we propose Counterfactual Routing (CoR), a training-free inference framework designed to awaken these dormant experts. CoR integrates layer-wise perturbation analysis with the Counterfactual Expert Impact (CEI) metric to dynamically shift computational resources from syntax-dominant to knowledge-intensive layers while maintaining a constant total activation count, effectively retrieving causally decisive experts via virtual ablation. Extensive experiments on TruthfulQA, FACTOR, and TriviaQA demonstrate that CoR improves factual accuracy by 3.1\% on average without increasing the inference budget, establishing a superior Pareto frontier compared to static scaling strategies.

摘要：稀疏的專家混合（MoE）模型已實現了顯著的可擴展性，但在處理長尾知識時仍然容易出現幻覺。我們發現這種脆弱性源於靜態的 Top-$k$ 路由：路由器傾向於偏好高頻模式而非稀有的事實關聯。因此，擁有關鍵長尾知識的「專家專家」經常被分配低的閘控分數，並保持「休眠」狀態——儘管它們在其他輸入上具有明顯的因果重要性，但在特定標記上卻被低估。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了反事實路由（CoR），這是一種無需訓練的推理框架，旨在喚醒這些休眠的專家。CoR 將層級擾動分析與反事實專家影響（CEI）指標結合，動態地將計算資源從語法主導的層轉移到知識密集的層，同時保持總激活計數不變，通過虛擬消融有效地檢索因果決定性的專家。在 TruthfulQA、FACTOR 和 TriviaQA 上的廣泛實驗表明，CoR 在不增加推理預算的情況下，平均提高了 3.1\% 的事實準確性，建立了與靜態擴展策略相比的優越 Pareto 邊界。

##### **SFT-GRPO Data Overlap as a Post-Training Hyperparameter for Autoformalization**
2604.13515v1 by Xiaole Su, Kasey Zhang, Andy Lyu

Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) followed by Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is a common post-training recipe. Keeping SFT and GRPO data disjoint consistently outperforms full overlap at zero additional compute cost. Evaluating on Gaokao-Formal and PutnamBench under both compile pass at k and semantic pass at k assessed by an LLM judge, we find that lower overlap is monotonically associated with higher compilation and semantic accuracy. At 0 percent overlap, GRPO yields a 10.4 percentage point semantic gain over SFT alone on Gaokao, while at 100 percent overlap both metrics remain flat, rendering the GRPO stage effectively redundant. We further show that dual-metric evaluation reveals compile semantic gaps exceeding 30 percentage points for the highest compiling models, a disparity invisible under compile-only benchmarking. To our knowledge, this is the first controlled investigation of SFT-GRPO data overlap as a post-training hyperparameter, demonstrating how model behavior varies based on the degree of data sharing between training stages.

##### **Towards Scalable Lightweight GUI Agents via Multi-role Orchestration**
2604.13488v1 by Ziwei Wang, Junjie Zheng, Leyang Yang, Sheng Zhou, Xiaoxuan Tang, Zhouhua Fang, Zhiwei Liu, Dajun Chen, Yong Li, Jiajun Bu

Autonomous Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents powered by Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) enable digital automation on end-user devices. While scaling both parameters and data has yielded substantial gains, advanced methods still suffer from prohibitive deployment costs on resource-constrained devices. ##### **Optimistic Policy Learning under Pessimistic Adversaries with Regret and Violation Guarantees**
2604.14243v2 by Sourav Ganguly, Kartik Pandit, Arnob Ghosh

Real-world decision-making systems operate in environments where state transitions depend not only on the agent's actions, but also on \textbf{exogenous factors outside its control}--competing agents, environmental disturbances, or strategic adversaries--formally, $s_{h+1} = f(s_h, a_h, \bar{a}_h)+ω_h$ where $\bar{a}_h$ is the adversary/external action, $a_h$ is the agent's action, and $ω_h$ is an additive noise. Ignoring such factors can yield policies that are optimal in isolation but \textbf{fail catastrophically in deployment}, particularly when safety constraints must be satisfied.
  Standard Constrained MDP formulations assume the agent is the sole driver of state evolution, an assumption that breaks down in safety-critical settings. Existing robust RL approaches address this via distributional robustness over transition kernels, but do not explicitly model the \textbf{strategic interaction} between agent and exogenous factor, and rely on strong assumptions about divergence from a known nominal model.
  We model the exogenous factor as an \textbf{adversarial policy} $\barπ$ that co-determines state transitions, and ask how an agent can remain both optimal and safe against such an adversary. \emph{To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to study safety-constrained RL under explicit adversarial dynamics}. We propose \textbf{Robust Hallucinated Constrained Upper-Confidence RL} (\texttt{RHC-UCRL}), a model-based algorithm that maintains optimism over both agent and adversary policies, explicitly separating epistemic from aleatoric uncertainty. \texttt{RHC-UCRL} achieves sub-linear regret and constraint violation guarantees.

摘要：現實世界的決策系統在環境中運作，其中狀態轉換不僅依賴於代理的行動，還依賴於\textbf{超出其控制的外部因素}——競爭代理、環境擾動或戰略對手——形式上，$s_{h+1} = f(s_h, a_h, \bar{a}_h)+ω_h$，其中$\bar{a}_h$是對手/外部行動，$a_h$是代理的行動，而$ω_h$是附加噪聲。忽略這些因素可能會產生在孤立情況下最佳的政策，但在實施時\textbf{會災難性失敗}，特別是在必須滿足安全約束的情況下。  
標準的受約束MDP公式假設代理是狀態演變的唯一驅動者，這一假設在安全關鍵的環境中會失效。現有的穩健強化學習方法通過對轉移核的分佈穩健性來解決這個問題，但並未明確建模代理與外部因素之間的\textbf{戰略互動}，並依賴於對已知標稱模型的偏離的強假設。  
我們將外部因素建模為\textbf{對抗性政策} $\barπ$，該政策共同決定狀態轉換，並詢問代理如何能夠在面對這樣的對手時保持最佳和安全。\emph{據我們所知，這是第一個研究在明確對抗動態下的安全受約束強化學習的工作}。我們提出\textbf{穩健幻覺受約束上置信強化學習} (\texttt{RHC-UCRL})，這是一種基於模型的算法，對代理和對手政策保持樂觀，明確區分認知不確定性和隨機不確定性。\texttt{RHC-UCRL}實現了次線性悔恨和約束違反保證。

##### **From Relevance to Authority: Authority-aware Generative Retrieval in Web Search Engines**
2604.13468v1 by Sunkyung Lee, Jihye Back, Donghyeon Jeon, Soonhwan Kwon, Moonkwon Kim, Inho Kang, Jongwuk Lee

Generative information retrieval (GenIR) formulates the retrieval process as a text-to-text generation task, leveraging the vast knowledge of large language models. However, existing works primarily optimize for relevance while often overlooking document trustworthiness. This is critical in high-stakes domains like healthcare and finance, where relying solely on semantic relevance risks retrieving unreliable information. To address this, we propose an Authority-aware Generative Retriever (AuthGR), the first framework that incorporates authority into GenIR. AuthGR consists of three key components: (i) Multimodal Authority Scoring, which employs a vision-language model to quantify authority from textual and visual cues; (ii) a Three-stage Training Pipeline to progressively instill authority awareness into the retriever; and (iii) a Hybrid Ensemble Pipeline for robust deployment. Offline evaluations demonstrate that AuthGR successfully enhances both authority and accuracy, with our 3B model matching a 14B baseline. Crucially, large-scale online A/B tests and human evaluations conducted on the commercial web search platform confirm significant improvements in real-world user engagement and reliability.

摘要：生成信息检索（GenIR）将检索过程表述为文本到文本的生成任务，利用大型语言模型的广泛知识。<lb/>然而，现有的工作主要优化相关性，往往忽视文档的可信度。<lb/>在医疗和金融等高风险领域，这一点至关重要，因为仅依赖语义相关性可能会检索到不可靠的信息。<lb/>为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种关注权威性的生成检索器（AuthGR），这是第一个将权威性纳入GenIR的框架。<lb/>AuthGR由三个关键组件组成：<lb/>(i) 多模态权威评分，利用视觉语言模型从文本和视觉线索中量化权威性；<lb/>(ii) 三阶段训练管道，逐步将权威意识灌输到检索器中；<lb/>(iii) 混合集成管道，用于稳健部署。<lb/>离线评估表明，AuthGR成功增强了权威性和准确性，我们的3B模型与14B基线相匹配。<lb/>至关重要的是，在商业网络搜索平台上进行的大规模在线A/B测试和人工评估证实了在实际用户参与度和可靠性方面的显著改善。

##### **Outperforming Self-Attention Mechanisms in Solar Irradiance Forecasting via Physics-Guided Neural Networks**
2604.13455v1 by Mohammed Ezzaldin Babiker Abdullah, Rufaidah Abdallah Ibrahim Mohammed

Accurate Global Horizontal Irradiance (GHI) forecasting is critical for grid stability, particularly in arid regions characterized by rapid aerosol fluctuations. While recent trends favor computationally expensive Transformer-based architectures, this paper challenges the prevailing "complexity-first" paradigm. We propose a lightweight, Physics-Informed Hybrid CNN-BiLSTM framework that prioritizes domain knowledge over architectural depth. The model integrates a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) for spatial feature extraction with a Bi-Directional LSTM for capturing temporal dependencies. Unlike standard data-driven approaches, our model is explicitly guided by a vector of 15 engineered features including Clear-Sky indices and Solar Zenith Angle - rather than relying solely on raw historical data. Hyperparameters are rigorously tuned using Bayesian Optimization to ensure global optimality. Experimental validation using NASA POWER data in Sudan demonstrates that our physics-guided approach achieves a Root Mean Square Error (RMSE) of 19.53 W/m^2, significantly outperforming complex attention-based baselines (RMSE 30.64 W/m^2). These results confirm a "Complexity Paradox": in high-noise meteorological tasks, explicit physical constraints offer a more efficient and accurate alternative to self-attention mechanisms. The findings advocate for a shift towards hybrid, physics-aware AI for real-time renewable energy management.

摘要：準確的全球水平輻射 (GHI) 預測對於電網穩定性至關重要，特別是在特徵為快速氣溶膠波動的乾旱地區。雖然近期趨勢偏向計算成本高昂的基於Transformer的架構，但本文挑戰了現行的「複雜性優先」範式。我們提出了一個輕量級的物理知識驅動混合 CNN-BiLSTM 框架，優先考慮領域知識而非架構深度。該模型整合了卷積神經網絡 (CNN) 用於空間特徵提取，並使用雙向 LSTM 捕捉時間依賴性。與標準的數據驅動方法不同，我們的模型明確地受到15個工程特徵的指導，包括晴空指數和太陽天頂角，而不是僅僅依賴原始歷史數據。超參數經過嚴格調整，使用貝葉斯優化以確保全局最優性。使用 NASA POWER 數據在蘇丹進行的實驗驗證顯示，我們的物理引導方法達到了 19.53 W/m^2 的均方根誤差 (RMSE)，顯著優於複雜的基於注意力的基準 (RMSE 30.64 W/m^2)。這些結果確認了一個「複雜性悖論」：在高噪聲氣象任務中，明確的物理約束提供了一種比自注意力機制更高效且準確的替代方案。這些發現倡導向混合的、具有物理意識的人工智慧轉變，以實現即時可再生能源管理。

##### **Minimax Optimality and Spectral Routing for Majority-Vote Ensembles under Markov Dependence**
2604.13414v1 by Ibne Farabi Shihab, Sanjeda Akter, Anuj Sharma

Majority-vote ensembles achieve variance reduction by averaging over diverse, approximately independent base learners. When training data exhibits Markov dependence, as in time-series forecasting, reinforcement learning (RL) replay buffers, and spatial grids, this classical guarantee degrades in ways that existing theory does not fully quantify. We provide a minimax characterization of this phenomenon for discrete classification in a fixed-dimensional Markov setting, together with an adaptive algorithm that matches the rate on a graph-regular subclass. We first establish an information-theoretic lower bound for stationary, reversible, geometrically ergodic chains in fixed ambient dimension, showing that no measurable estimator can achieve excess classification risk better than $Ω(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$. We then prove that, on the AR(1) witness subclass underlying the lower-bound construction, dependence-agnostic uniform bagging is provably suboptimal with excess risk bounded below by $Ω(\Tmix/\sqrt{n})$, exhibiting a $\sqrt{\Tmix}$ algorithmic gap. Finally, we propose \emph{adaptive spectral routing}, which partitions the training data via the empirical Fiedler eigenvector of a dependency graph and achieves the minimax rate $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$ up to a lower-order geometric cut term on a graph-regular subclass, without knowledge of $\Tmix$. Experiments on synthetic Markov chains, 2D spatial grids, the 128-dataset UCR archive, and Atari DQN ensembles validate the theoretical predictions. Consequences for deep RL target variance, scalability via Nyström approximation, and bounded non-stationarity are developed as supporting material in the appendix.

摘要：大多數投票集成通過對多樣化、近似獨立的基學習者進行平均來實現方差降低。當訓練數據顯示馬爾可夫依賴性時，例如在時間序列預測、強化學習（RL）重播緩衝區和空間網格中，這一經典保證會以現有理論未能完全量化的方式退化。我們為固定維度馬爾可夫設定中的離散分類提供了這一現象的最小最大特徵描述，並提出了一種自適應算法，該算法在圖正則子類上匹配速率。我們首先為固定環境維度中的平穩、可逆、幾何遍歷鏈建立了一個信息論下界，顯示出沒有可測估計量能夠實現超額分類風險優於 $Ω(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$。然後，我們證明在支持下界構造的 AR(1) 目擊子類上，與依賴無關的均勻包裝在超額風險下界為 $Ω(\Tmix/\sqrt{n})$ 的情況下，顯示出一個 $\sqrt{\Tmix}$ 的算法差距。最後，我們提出了 \emph{自適應光譜路由}，該方法通過依賴圖的經驗 Fiedler 特徵向量對訓練數據進行劃分，並在圖正則子類上達到最小最大速率 $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$，而無需知道 $\Tmix$。對合成馬爾可夫鏈、2D 空間網格、128 數據集 UCR 存檔和 Atari DQN 集成的實驗驗證了理論預測。附錄中發展了對深度 RL 目標方差、通過 Nyström 近似的可擴展性和有界非平穩性的影響作為支持材料。

##### **Empirical Evidence of Complexity-Induced Limits in Large Language Models on Finite Discrete State-Space Problems with Explicit Validity Constraints**
2604.13371v1 by Md. Fahad Ullah Utsho, Mohd. Ruhul Ameen, Akif Islam, Md. Golam Rashed, Dipankar Das

Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly described as possessing strong reasoning capabilities, supported by high performance on mathematical, logical, and planning benchmarks. However, most existing evaluations rely on aggregate accuracy over fixed datasets, obscuring how reasoning behavior evolves as task complexity increases. In this work, we introduce a controlled benchmarking framework to systematically evaluate the robustness of reasoning in Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) under progressively increasing problem complexity. We construct a suite of nine classical reasoning tasks: Boolean Satisfiability, Cryptarithmetic, Graph Coloring, River Crossing, Tower of Hanoi, Water Jug, Checker Jumping, Sudoku, and Rubik's Cube, each parameterized to precisely control complexity while preserving underlying semantics. Using deterministic validators, we evaluate multiple open and proprietary LRMs across low, intermediate, and high complexity regimes, ensuring that only fully valid solutions are accepted. Our results reveal a consistent phase transition like behavior: models achieve high accuracy at low complexity but degrade sharply beyond task specific complexity thresholds. We formalize this phenomenon as reasoning collapse. Across tasks, we observe substantial accuracy declines, often exceeding 50%, accompanied by inconsistent reasoning traces, constraint violations, loss of state tracking, and confidently incorrect outputs. Increased reasoning length does not reliably improve correctness, and gains in one problem family do not generalize to others. These findings highlight the need for evaluation methodologies that move beyond static benchmarks and explicitly measure reasoning robustness under controlled complexity.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越被描述為具備強大的推理能力，這一點得到了在數學、邏輯和規劃基準測試中高性能的支持。然而，大多數現有的評估依賴於固定數據集上的總體準確性，掩蓋了隨著任務複雜性增加而推理行為的演變。在本研究中，我們引入了一個受控的基準測試框架，以系統地評估大型推理模型（LRMs）在逐步增加的問題複雜性下的推理穩健性。我們構建了一套九個經典推理任務：布爾滿足性、密碼算術、圖著色、過河、漢諾塔、水壺、跳棋、數獨和魔方，每個任務都經過參數化以精確控制複雜性，同時保留基本語義。使用確定性驗證器，我們在低、中、高複雜性範疇中評估多個開放和專有的LRMs，確保只有完全有效的解決方案被接受。我們的結果顯示出一致的相變行為：模型在低複雜性下達到高準確性，但在超過特定任務複雜性閾值後急劇下降。我們將這一現象形式化為推理崩潰。在各個任務中，我們觀察到顯著的準確性下降，往往超過50%，伴隨著不一致的推理痕跡、約束違反、狀態追踪的喪失以及自信錯誤的輸出。推理長度的增加並不可靠地改善正確性，且在一個問題家族中的增益並不會推廣到其他問題。這些發現突顯了需要超越靜態基準的評估方法論，並明確測量在受控複雜性下的推理穩健性。

##### **Finetuning-Free Diffusion Model with Adaptive Constraint Guidance for Inorganic Crystal Structure Generation**

The discovery of inorganic crystal structures with targeted properties is a significant challenge in materials science. Generative models, especially state-of-the-art diffusion models, offer the promise of modeling complex data distributions and proposing novel, realistic samples. However, current generative AI models still struggle to produce diverse, original, and reliable structures of experimentally achievable materials suitable for high-stakes applications.
  In this work, we propose a generative machine learning framework based on diffusion models with adaptive constraint guidance, which enables the incorporation of user-defined physical and chemical constraints during the generation process. This approach is designed to be practical and interpretable for human experts, allowing transparent decision-making and expert-driven exploration. To ensure the robustness and validity of the generated candidates, we introduce a multi-step validation pipeline that combines graph neural network estimators trained to achieve DFT-level accuracy and convex hull analysis for assessing thermodynamic stability. ##### **AgentSPEX: An Agent SPecification and EXecution Language**
2604.13346v1 by Pengcheng Wang, Jerry Huang, Jiarui Yao, Rui Pan, Peizhi Niu, Yaowenqi Liu, Ruida Wang, Renhao Lu, Yuwei Guo, Tong Zhang

Language-model agent systems commonly rely on reactive prompting, in which a single instruction guides the model through an open-ended sequence of reasoning and tool-use steps, leaving control flow and intermediate state implicit and making agent behavior potentially difficult to control. Orchestration frameworks such as LangGraph, DSPy, and CrewAI impose greater structure through explicit workflow definitions, but tightly couple workflow logic with Python, making agents difficult to maintain and modify. In this paper, we introduce AgentSPEX, an Agent SPecification and EXecution Language for specifying LLM-agent workflows with explicit control flow and modular structure, along with a customizable agent harness. AgentSPEX supports typed steps, branching and loops, parallel execution, reusable submodules, and explicit state management, and these workflows execute within an agent harness that provides tool access, a sandboxed virtual environment, and support for checkpointing, verification, and logging. Furthermore, we provide a visual editor with synchronized graph and workflow views for authoring and inspection. We include ready-to-use agents for deep research and scientific research, and we evaluate AgentSPEX on 7 benchmarks. Finally, we show through a user study that AgentSPEX provides a more interpretable and accessible workflow-authoring paradigm than a popular existing agent framework.

摘要：語言模型代理系統通常依賴反應式提示，其中單一指令引導模型通過開放式的推理和工具使用步驟，留下控制流程和中間狀態隱含，使得代理行為可能難以控制。像 LangGraph、DSPy 和 CrewAI 這樣的協調框架通過明確的工作流程定義施加更大的結構，但將工作流程邏輯與 Python 緊密耦合，使得代理難以維護和修改。在本文中，我們介紹了 AgentSPEX，一種代理規範和執行語言，用於指定具有明確控制流程和模組化結構的 LLM-代理工作流程，以及一個可自定義的代理工具。AgentSPEX 支持類型化步驟、分支和循環、並行執行、可重用子模組和明確的狀態管理，這些工作流程在提供工具訪問、沙盒虛擬環境以及支持檢查點、驗證和日誌記錄的代理工具內執行。此外，我們提供了一個具有同步圖形和工作流程視圖的可視化編輯器，用於創作和檢查。我們包括了可即用的代理，用於深入研究和科學研究，並在 7 個基準上評估了 AgentSPEX。最後，我們通過用戶研究顯示，AgentSPEX 提供了一種比流行的現有代理框架更具可解釋性和可訪問性的工作流程創作範式。

##### **WebXSkill: Skill Learning for Autonomous Web Agents**
2604.13318v1 by Zhaoyang Wang, Qianhui Wu, Xuchao Zhang, Chaoyun Zhang, Wenlin Yao, Fazle Elahi Faisal, Baolin Peng, Si Qin, Suman Nath, Qingwei Lin, Chetan Bansal, Dongmei Zhang, Saravan Rajmohan, Jianfeng Gao, Huaxiu Yao

Autonomous web agents powered by large language models (LLMs) have shown promise in completing complex browser tasks, yet they still struggle with long-horizon workflows. A key bottleneck is the grounding gap in existing skill formulations: textual workflow skills provide natural language guidance but cannot be directly executed, while code-based skills are executable but opaque to the agent, offering no step-level understanding for error recovery or adaptation. We introduce WebXSkill, a framework that bridges this gap with executable skills, each pairing a parameterized action program with step-level natural language guidance, enabling both direct execution and agent-driven adaptation. WebXSkill operates in three stages: skill extraction mines reusable action subsequences from readily available synthetic agent trajectories and abstracts them into parameterized skills, skill organization indexes skills into a URL-based graph for context-aware retrieval, and skill deployment exposes two complementary modes, grounded mode for fully automated multi-step execution and guided mode where skills serve as step-by-step instructions that the agent follows with its native planning. On WebArena and WebVoyager, WebXSkill improves task success rate by up to 9.8 and 12.9 points over the baseline, respectively, demonstrating the effectiveness of executable skills for web agents. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/WebXSkill.

摘要：自主網頁代理商由大型語言模型（LLMs）驅動，已顯示出在完成複雜瀏覽器任務方面的潛力，但在長期工作流程上仍然面臨挑戰。一個主要的瓶頸是現有技能表述中的基礎差距：文本工作流程技能提供自然語言指導，但無法直接執行，而基於代碼的技能則可執行但對代理商來說不透明，無法提供逐步的理解以進行錯誤恢復或適應。我們介紹了WebXSkill，這是一個通過可執行技能彌合這一差距的框架，每個技能將參數化的動作程序與逐步的自然語言指導配對，使得既能直接執行又能進行代理驅動的適應。WebXSkill運作分為三個階段：技能提取從現成的合成代理軌跡中挖掘可重用的動作子序列並將其抽象為參數化技能，技能組織將技能索引到基於URL的圖中以便於上下文感知的檢索，技能部署則提供兩種互補模式，基於基礎的模式用於完全自動化的多步執行，而指導模式則將技能作為代理商依據其本地規劃遵循的逐步指令。在WebArena和WebVoyager上，WebXSkill分別提高了任務成功率高達9.8和12.9個百分點，展示了可執行技能對網頁代理商的有效性。代碼可在https://github.com/aiming-lab/WebXSkill公開獲得。

##### **Graph-Based Fraud Detection with Dual-Path Graph Filtering**
2604.14235v1 by Wei He, Wensheng Gan, Philip S. Yu

Fraud detection on graph data can be viewed as a demanding task that requires distinguishing between different types of nodes. Because graph neural networks (GNNs) are naturally suited for processing information encoded in graph form through their message-passing operations, methods based on GNN models have increasingly attracted attention in the fraud detection domain. However, fraud graphs inherently exhibit relation camouflage, high heterophily, and class imbalance, causing most GNNs to underperform in fraud detection tasks. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a Graph-Based Fraud Detection Model with Dual-Path Graph Filtering (DPF-GFD). DPF-GFD first applies a beta wavelet-based operator to the original graph to capture key structural patterns. It then constructs a similarity graph from distance-based node representations and applies an improved low-pass filter. The embeddings from the original and similarity graphs are fused through supervised representation learning to obtain node features, which are finally used by an ensemble tree model to assess the fraud risk of unlabeled nodes. Unlike existing single-graph smoothing approaches, DPF-GFD introduces a frequency-complementary dual-path filtering paradigm tailored for fraud detection, explicitly decoupling structural anomaly modeling and feature similarity modeling. This design enables more discriminative and stable node representations in highly heterophilous and imbalanced fraud graphs. Comprehensive experiments on four real-world financial fraud detection datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of our proposed method.

摘要：詐騙檢測在圖形數據上可以被視為一項要求高的任務，需要區分不同類型的節點。由於圖神經網絡（GNNs）自然適合通過其消息傳遞操作處理以圖形形式編碼的信息，因此基於GNN模型的方法在詐騙檢測領域越來越受到關注。然而，詐騙圖本質上表現出關係偽裝、高異質性和類別不平衡，導致大多數GNN在詐騙檢測任務中表現不佳。為了解決這些挑戰，本文提出了一種基於圖的雙通路圖過濾詐騙檢測模型（DPF-GFD）。DPF-GFD首先對原始圖應用基於貝塔小波的運算符，以捕捉關鍵的結構模式。然後，它從基於距離的節點表示構建相似圖，並應用改進的低通濾波器。來自原始圖和相似圖的嵌入通過監督式表示學習進行融合，以獲得節點特徵，這些特徵最終由集成樹模型用於評估未標記節點的詐騙風險。與現有的單圖平滑方法不同，DPF-GFD引入了一種針對詐騙檢測量身定制的頻率互補雙通路過濾範式，明確解耦結構異常建模和特徵相似性建模。這一設計使得在高度異質和不平衡的詐騙圖中能夠實現更具區分性和穩定性的節點表示。在四個現實世界的金融詐騙檢測數據集上的綜合實驗證明了我們提出的方法的有效性。

##### **Optimizing Earth Observation Satellite Schedules under Unknown Operational Constraints: An Active Constraint Acquisition Approach**
2604.13283v1 by Mohamed-Bachir Belaid

Earth Observation (EO) satellite scheduling (deciding which imaging tasks to perform and when) is a well-studied combinatorial optimization problem. Existing methods typically assume that the operational constraint model is fully specified in advance. In practice, however, constraints governing separation between observations, power budgets, and thermal limits are often embedded in engineering artefacts or high-fidelity simulators rather than in explicit mathematical models. We study EO scheduling under \emph{unknown constraints}: the objective is known, but feasibility must be learned interactively from a binary oracle. Working with a simplified model restricted to pairwise separation and global capacity constraints, we introduce Conservative Constraint Acquisition~(CCA), a domain-specific procedure designed to identify justified constraints efficiently in practice while limiting unnecessary tightening of the learned model. Embedded in the \textsc{Learn\&Optimize} framework, CCA supports an interactive search process that alternates optimization under a learned constraint model with targeted oracle queries. On synthetic instances with up to 50~tasks and dense constraint networks, L\&O improves over a no-knowledge greedy baseline and uses far fewer main oracle queries than a two-phase acquire-then-solve baseline (FAO). For $n\leq 30$, the average gap drops from 65--68\% (Priority Greedy) to 17.7--35.8\% using L\&O. At $n{=}50$, where the CP-SAT reference is the best feasible solution found in 120~s, L\&O improves on FAO on average (17.9\% vs.\ 20.3\%) while using 21.3 main queries instead of 100 and about $5\times$ less execution time.

摘要：地球觀測（EO）衛星排程（決定執行哪些成像任務及何時執行）是一個研究已久的組合優化問題。現有的方法通常假設操作約束模型在事前已完全指定。然而，在實際操作中，控制觀測之間分隔、功率預算和熱限制的約束往往嵌入在工程文檔或高保真模擬器中，而不是在明確的數學模型中。我們研究在\emph{未知約束}下的EO排程：目標是已知的，但可行性必須通過與二元神諭的互動學習來獲得。在一個簡化模型中，限制在成對分隔和全局容量約束，我們引入了保守約束獲取（CCA），這是一種特定於領域的程序，旨在有效識別合理的約束，同時限制學習模型的不必要收緊。CCA嵌入在\textsc{Learn\&Optimize}框架中，支持一個互動搜索過程，該過程在學習的約束模型下進行優化，並與針對性的神諭查詢交替進行。在最多有50個任務和密集約束網絡的合成實例中，L\&O在無知貪婪基線上有所改善，並且使用的主要神諭查詢比兩階段的獲取然後解決基線（FAO）少得多。對於$n\leq 30$，平均差距從65--68\%（優先貪婪）下降到17.7--35.8\%，使用L\&O。在$n{=}50$的情況下，CP-SAT參考是120秒內找到的最佳可行解，L\&O在FAO上平均改善（17.9\%對20.3\%），同時使用21.3個主要查詢而不是100個，執行時間約少了$5\times$。

##### **Lazy or Efficient? Towards Accessible Eye-Tracking Event Detection Using LLMs**
2604.13243v1 by Dongyang Guo, Yasmeen Abdrabou, Enkelejda Kasneci

Gaze event detection is fundamental to vision science, human-computer interaction, and applied analytics. However, current workflows often require specialized programming knowledge and careful handling of heterogeneous raw data formats. Classical detectors such as I-VT and I-DT are effective but highly sensitive to preprocessing and parameterization, limiting their usability outside specialized laboratories. This work introduces a code-free, large language model (LLM)-driven pipeline that converts natural language instructions into an end-to-end analysis. The system (1) inspects raw eye-tracking files to infer structure and metadata, (2) generates executable routines for data cleaning and detector implementation from concise user prompts, (3) applies the generated detector to label fixations and saccades, and (4) returns results and explanatory reports, and allows users to iteratively optimize their code by editing the prompt. ##### **SemiFA: An Agentic Multi-Modal Framework for Autonomous Semiconductor Failure Analysis Report Generation**
2604.13236v1 by Shivam Chand Kaushik

Semiconductor failure analysis (FA) requires engineers to examine inspection images, correlate equipment telemetry, consult historical defect records, and write structured reports, a process that can consume several hours of expert time per case. We present SemiFA, an agentic multi-modal framework that autonomously generates structured FA reports from semiconductor inspection images in under one minute. SemiFA decomposes FA into a four-agent LangGraph pipeline: a DefectDescriber that classifies and narrates defect morphology using DINOv2 and LLaVA-1.6, a RootCauseAnalyzer that fuses SECS/GEM equipment telemetry with historically similar defects retrieved from a Qdrant vector database, a SeverityClassifier that assigns severity and estimates yield impact, and a RecipeAdvisor that proposes corrective process adjustments. A fifth node assembles a PDF report. We introduce SemiFA-930, a dataset of 930 annotated semiconductor defect images paired with structured FA narratives across nine defect classes, drawn from procedural synthesis, WM-811K, and MixedWM38. Our DINOv2-based classifier achieves 92.1% accuracy on 140 validation images (macro F1 = 0.917), and the full pipeline produces complete FA reports in 48 seconds on an NVIDIA A100-SXM4-40 GB GPU. A GPT-4o judge ablation across four modality conditions demonstrates that multi-modal fusion improves root cause reasoning by +0.86 composite points (1-5 scale) over an image-only baseline, with equipment telemetry as the more load-bearing modality. To our knowledge, SemiFA is the first system to integrate SECS/GEM equipment telemetry into a vision-language model pipeline for autonomous FA report generation.

摘要：半導體失效分析（FA）要求工程師檢查檢驗影像，關聯設備遙測，查閱歷史缺陷記錄，並撰寫結構化報告，這一過程可能會消耗每個案例數小時的專家時間。<lb/>我們提出了SemiFA，一個自主生成結構化FA報告的多模態框架，能在不到一分鐘的時間內從半導體檢驗影像中生成報告。<lb/>SemiFA將FA分解為四個代理的LangGraph管道：一個DefectDescriber使用DINOv2和LLaVA-1.6來分類和敘述缺陷形態，一個RootCauseAnalyzer將SECS/GEM設備遙測與從Qdrant向量數據庫檢索到的歷史相似缺陷融合，一個SeverityClassifier分配嚴重性並估算產量影響，還有一個RecipeAdvisor提出修正的過程調整。<lb/>第五個節點組裝PDF報告。<lb/>我們介紹了SemiFA-930，一個包含930個註解的半導體缺陷影像資料集，這些影像與九個缺陷類別的結構化FA敘述配對，來源於程序合成、WM-811K和MixedWM38。<lb/>我們基於DINOv2的分類器在140個驗證影像上達到92.1%的準確率（宏觀F1 = 0.917），而整個管道在NVIDIA A100-SXM4-40 GB GPU上能在48秒內生成完整的FA報告。<lb/>一個GPT-4o的評審在四種模態條件下的消融實驗顯示，多模態融合使根本原因推理在1-5的評分標準上提高了+0.86的綜合分數，設備遙測作為更具承載能力的模態。<lb/>據我們所知，SemiFA是第一個將SECS/GEM設備遙測整合進視覺-語言模型管道以實現自主FA報告生成的系統。

#### Abstracts
##### **ASMR-Bench: Auditing for Sabotage in ML Research**
2604.16286v1 by Eric Gan, Aryan Bhatt, Buck Shlegeris, Julian Stastny, Vivek Hebbar

As AI systems are increasingly used to conduct research autonomously, misaligned systems could introduce subtle flaws that produce misleading results while evading detection. We introduce ASMR-Bench (Auditing for Sabotage in ML Research), a benchmark for evaluating the ability of auditors to detect sabotage in ML research codebases. ASMR-Bench consists of 9 ML research codebases with sabotaged variants that produce qualitatively different experimental results. Each sabotage modifies implementation details, such as hyperparameters, training data, or evaluation code, while preserving the high-level methodology described in the paper. We evaluated frontier LLMs and LLM-assisted human auditors on ASMR-Bench and found that both struggled to reliably detect sabotage: the best performance was an AUROC of 0.77 and a top-1 fix rate of 42%, achieved by Gemini 3.1 Pro. We also tested LLMs as red teamers and found that LLM-generated sabotages were weaker than human-generated ones but still sometimes evaded same-capability LLM auditors. We release ASMR-Bench to support research on monitoring and auditing techniques for AI-conducted research.

摘要：隨著 AI 系統越來越多地被用來自主進行研究，未對齊的系統可能會引入微妙的缺陷，從而產生誤導性的結果而不被檢測到。我們介紹 ASMR-Bench（機器學習研究中的破壞審計），這是一個用於評估審計員檢測機器學習研究代碼庫中破壞能力的基準。ASMR-Bench 包含 9 個機器學習研究代碼庫，並具有產生質量上不同實驗結果的破壞變體。每個破壞都修改了實現細節，例如超參數、訓練數據或評估代碼，同時保留了論文中描述的高層次方法論。我們在 ASMR-Bench 上評估了前沿的 LLM 和 LLM 輔助的人類審計員，發現兩者都難以可靠地檢測破壞：最佳表現是 AUROC 0.77 和 42% 的前 1 修復率，由 Gemini 3.1 Pro 實現。我們還測試了 LLM 作為紅隊成員，發現 LLM 生成的破壞比人類生成的弱，但有時仍能逃避同等能力的 LLM 審計員。我們發布 ASMR-Bench 以支持對 AI 進行研究的監控和審計技術的研究。

##### **Using Large Language Models and Knowledge Graphs to Improve the Interpretability of Machine Learning Models in Manufacturing**
2604.16280v1 by Thomas Bayer, Alexander Lohr, Sarah Weiß, Bernd Michelberger, Wolfram Höpken

Explaining Machine Learning (ML) results in a transparent and user-friendly manner remains a challenging task of Explainable Artificial Intelligence (XAI). In this paper, we present a method to enhance the interpretability of ML models by using a Knowledge Graph (KG). We store domain-specific data along with ML results and their corresponding explanations, establishing a structured connection between domain knowledge and ML insights. To make these insights accessible to users, we designed a selective retrieval method in which relevant triplets are extracted from the KG and processed by a Large Language Model (LLM) to generate user-friendly explanations of ML results. We evaluated our method in a manufacturing environment using the XAI Question Bank. Beyond standard questions, we introduce more complex, tailored questions that highlight the strengths of our approach. We evaluated 33 questions, analyzing responses using quantitative metrics such as accuracy and consistency, as well as qualitative ones such as clarity and usefulness. Our contribution is both theoretical and practical: from a theoretical perspective, we present a novel approach for effectively enabling LLMs to dynamically access a KG in order to improve the explainability of ML results. From a practical perspective, we provide empirical evidence showing that such explanations can be successfully applied in real-world manufacturing environments, supporting better decision-making in manufacturing processes.

摘要：解釋機器學習（ML）結果以透明且使用者友好的方式仍然是可解釋人工智慧（XAI）的一項挑戰性任務。在本文中，我們提出了一種通過使用知識圖譜（KG）來增強ML模型可解釋性的方法。我們儲存領域特定的數據以及ML結果及其相應的解釋，建立領域知識與ML見解之間的結構化連結。為了使這些見解對使用者可訪問，我們設計了一種選擇性檢索方法，從KG中提取相關的三元組，並由大型語言模型（LLM）處理，以生成使用者友好的ML結果解釋。我們在製造環境中使用XAI問題庫評估我們的方法。除了標準問題外，我們還引入了更複雜、量身定制的問題，以突顯我們方法的優勢。我們評估了33個問題，使用準確性和一致性等定量指標，以及清晰度和有用性等定性指標來分析回應。我們的貢獻既具有理論性也具有實踐性：從理論的角度來看，我們提出了一種新穎的方法，能夠有效地使LLM動態訪問KG，以改善ML結果的可解釋性。從實踐的角度來看，我們提供了實證證據，顯示這樣的解釋可以成功應用於現實世界的製造環境中，支持更好的製造過程決策。

##### **Learning to Reason with Insight for Informal Theorem Proving**
2604.16278v1 by Yunhe Li, Hao Shi, Bowen Deng, Wei Wang, Mengzhe Ruan, Hanxu Hou, Zhongxiang Dai, Siyang Gao, Chao Wang, Shuang Qiu, Linqi Song

Although most of the automated theorem-proving approaches depend on formal proof systems, informal theorem proving can align better with large language models' (LLMs) strength in natural language processing. In this work, we identify a primary bottleneck in informal theorem proving as a lack of insight, namely the difficulty of recognizing the core techniques required to solve complex problems. To address this, we propose a novel framework designed to cultivate this essential reasoning skill and enable LLMs to perform insightful reasoning. We propose $\mathtt{DeepInsightTheorem}$, a hierarchical dataset that structures informal proofs by explicitly extracting core techniques and proof sketches alongside the final proof. To fully exploit this dataset, we design a Progressive Multi-Stage SFT strategy that mimics the human learning process, guiding the model from basic proof writing to insightful thinking. Our experiments on challenging mathematical benchmarks demonstrate that this insight-aware generation strategy significantly outperforms baselines. These results demonstrate that teaching models to identify and apply core techniques can substantially improve their mathematical reasoning.

摘要：雖然大多數自動定理證明方法依賴於形式證明系統，但非正式定理證明可以更好地與大型語言模型（LLMs）在自然語言處理方面的優勢對齊。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們確定了非正式定理證明中的一個主要瓶頸，即缺乏洞察力，特別是識別解決複雜問題所需核心技術的困難。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們提出了一個新穎的框架，旨在培養這一基本推理技能，使LLMs能夠進行有洞察力的推理。<lb/>我們提出了 $\mathtt{DeepInsightTheorem}$，這是一個層次化數據集，通過明確提取核心技術和證明草圖以及最終證明來結構化非正式證明。<lb/>為了充分利用這個數據集，我們設計了一個漸進式多階段SFT策略，模仿人類學習過程，指導模型從基本的證明寫作到有洞察力的思考。<lb/>我們在具有挑戰性的數學基準上的實驗表明，這種以洞察為導向的生成策略顯著優於基準。<lb/>這些結果表明，教導模型識別和應用核心技術可以顯著改善其數學推理能力。

##### **No Universal Courtesy: A Cross-Linguistic, Multi-Model Study of Politeness Effects on LLMs Using the PLUM Corpus**
2604.16275v1 by Hitesh Mehta, Arjit Saxena, Garima Chhikara, Rohit Kumar

This paper explores the response of Large Language Models (LLMs) to user prompts with different degrees of politeness and impoliteness. The Politeness Theory by Brown and Levinson and the Impoliteness Framework by Culpeper form the basis of experiments conducted across three languages (English, Hindi, Spanish), five models (Gemini-Pro, GPT-4o Mini, Claude 3.7 Sonnet, DeepSeek-Chat, and Llama 3), and three interaction histories between users (raw, polite, and impolite). Our sample consists of 22,500 pairs of prompts and responses of various types, evaluated across five levels of politeness using an eight-factor assessment framework: coherence, clarity, depth, responsiveness, context retention, toxicity, conciseness, and readability. The findings show that model performance is highly influenced by tone, dialogue history, and language. While polite prompts enhance the average response quality by up to ~11% and impolite tones worsen it, these effects are neither consistent nor universal across languages and models. English is best served by courteous or direct tones, Hindi by deferential and indirect tones, and Spanish by assertive tones. Among the models, Llama is the most tone-sensitive (11.5% range), whereas GPT is more robust to adversarial tone. These results indicate that politeness is a quantifiable computational variable that affects LLM behaviour, though its impact is language- and model-dependent rather than universal. To support reproducibility and future work, we additionally release PLUM (Politeness Levels in Utterances, Multilingual), a publicly available corpus of 1,500 human-validated prompts across three languages and five politeness categories, and provide a formal supplementary analysis of six falsifiable hypotheses derived from politeness theory, empirically assessed against the dataset.

摘要：這篇論文探討大型語言模型（LLMs）對不同程度的禮貌和不禮貌用戶提示的反應。布朗和萊文森的禮貌理論以及卡爾佩珀的不禮貌框架構成了在三種語言（英語、印地語、西班牙語）、五個模型（Gemini-Pro、GPT-4o Mini、Claude 3.7 Sonnet、DeepSeek-Chat 和 Llama 3）以及三種用戶互動歷史（原始、禮貌和不禮貌）中進行實驗的基礎。我們的樣本包含22,500對各種類型的提示和回應，並使用八個因素的評估框架在五個禮貌水平上進行評估：連貫性、清晰度、深度、反應性、上下文保留、毒性、簡潔性和可讀性。研究結果顯示，模型性能受到語氣、對話歷史和語言的高度影響。雖然禮貌的提示使平均回應質量提高了約11%，而不禮貌的語氣則使其惡化，但這些效果在不同語言和模型中並不一致或普遍。英語最適合使用禮貌或直接的語氣，印地語則適合使用恭敬和間接的語氣，而西班牙語則適合使用果斷的語氣。在這些模型中，Llama對語氣最敏感（範圍為11.5%），而GPT對對抗性語氣則更具穩健性。這些結果表明，禮貌是一個可量化的計算變量，影響LLM的行為，儘管其影響是依賴於語言和模型，而非普遍適用。為了支持可重複性和未來的研究，我們還發布了PLUM（語句中的禮貌水平，多語言），這是一個公開可用的語料庫，包含1,500個經人類驗證的提示，涵蓋三種語言和五個禮貌類別，並提供了基於禮貌理論衍生的六個可證偽假設的正式補充分析，這些假設經過實證評估與數據集進行比較。

##### **VEFX-Bench: A Holistic Benchmark for Generic Video Editing and Visual Effects**
2604.16272v1 by Xiangbo Gao, Sicong Jiang, Bangya Liu, Xinghao Chen, Minglai Yang, Siyuan Yang, Mingyang Wu, Jiongze Yu, Qi Zheng, Haozhi Wang, Jiayi Zhang, Jared Yang, Jie Yang, Zihan Wang, Qing Yin, Zhengzhong Tu

As AI-assisted video creation becomes increasingly practical, instruction-guided video editing has become essential for refining generated or captured footage to meet professional requirements. Yet the field still lacks both a large-scale human-annotated dataset with complete editing examples and a standardized evaluator for comparing editing systems. Existing resources are limited by small scale, missing edited outputs, or the absence of human quality labels, while current evaluation often relies on expensive manual inspection or generic vision-language model judges that are not specialized for editing quality. We introduce VEFX-Dataset, a human-annotated dataset containing 5,049 video editing examples across 9 major editing categories and 32 subcategories, each labeled along three decoupled dimensions: Instruction Following, Rendering Quality, and Edit Exclusivity. Building on VEFX-Dataset, we propose VEFX-Reward, a reward model designed specifically for video editing quality assessment. VEFX-Reward jointly processes the source video, the editing instruction, and the edited video, and predicts per-dimension quality scores via ordinal regression. We further release VEFX-Bench, a benchmark of 300 curated video-prompt pairs for standardized comparison of editing systems. Experiments show that VEFX-Reward aligns more strongly with human judgments than generic VLM judges and prior reward models on both standard IQA/VQA metrics and group-wise preference evaluation. Using VEFX-Reward as an evaluator, we benchmark representative commercial and open-source video editing systems, revealing a persistent gap between visual plausibility, instruction following, and edit locality in current models.

摘要：隨著AI輔助視頻創作變得越來越實用，指導性視頻編輯已成為精煉生成或捕獲的影像以滿足專業要求的必要條件。然而，該領域仍然缺乏一個大規模的人類標註數據集，該數據集包含完整的編輯示例，以及一個標準化的評估器來比較編輯系統。現有資源受到小規模、缺少編輯輸出或缺乏人類質量標籤的限制，而當前的評估通常依賴於昂貴的手動檢查或不專門針對編輯質量的通用視覺-語言模型評審。我們介紹VEFX-Dataset，一個人類標註的數據集，包含9個主要編輯類別和32個子類別中的5,049個視頻編輯示例，每個示例沿著三個解耦維度標註：指令遵循、渲染質量和編輯排他性。在VEFX-Dataset的基礎上，我們提出VEFX-Reward，一個專門為視頻編輯質量評估設計的獎勵模型。VEFX-Reward共同處理源視頻、編輯指令和編輯後視頻，並通過序數回歸預測每個維度的質量分數。我們進一步發布VEFX-Bench，一個包含300對策劃視頻-提示的基準，用於標準化比較編輯系統。實驗顯示，VEFX-Reward在標準IQA/VQA指標和群體偏好評估中，與人類判斷的對齊程度比通用VLM評審和先前的獎勵模型更強。使用VEFX-Reward作為評估器，我們對代表性的商業和開源視頻編輯系統進行基準測試，揭示了當前模型在視覺合理性、指令遵循和編輯局部性之間的持續差距。

##### **From Benchmarking to Reasoning: A Dual-Aspect, Large-Scale Evaluation of LLMs on Vietnamese Legal Text**
2604.16270v1 by Van-Truong Le

The complexity of Vietnam's legal texts presents a significant barrier to public access to justice. While Large Language Models offer a promising solution for legal text simplification, evaluating their true capabilities requires a multifaceted approach that goes beyond surface-level metrics. This paper introduces a comprehensive dual-aspect evaluation framework to address this need. First, we establish a performance benchmark for four state-of-the-art large language models (GPT-4o, Claude 3 Opus, Gemini 1.5 Pro, and Grok-1) across three key dimensions: Accuracy, Readability, and Consistency. Second, to understand the "why" behind these performance scores, we conduct a large-scale error analysis on a curated dataset of 60 complex Vietnamese legal articles, using a novel, expert-validated error typology. Our results reveal a crucial trade-off: models like Grok-1 excel in Readability and Consistency but compromise on fine-grained legal Accuracy, while models like Claude 3 Opus achieve high Accuracy scores that mask a significant number of subtle but critical reasoning errors. The error analysis pinpoints \textit{Incorrect Example} and \textit{Misinterpretation} as the most prevalent failures, confirming that the primary challenge for current LLMs is not summarization but controlled, accurate legal reasoning. By integrating a quantitative benchmark with a qualitative deep dive, our work provides a holistic and actionable assessment of LLMs for legal applications.

摘要：越南法律文本的複雜性對公眾獲取正義構成了重大障礙。雖然大型語言模型提供了一個有前景的法律文本簡化解決方案，但評估它們的真正能力需要一種多方面的方法，超越表面指標。本文介紹了一個全面的雙重評估框架來應對這一需求。首先，我們為四個最先進的大型語言模型（GPT-4o、Claude 3 Opus、Gemini 1.5 Pro 和 Grok-1）在三個關鍵維度上建立了一個性能基準：準確性、可讀性和一致性。其次，為了理解這些性能分數背後的“為什麼”，我們對一個精選的60篇複雜越南法律條款數據集進行了大規模的錯誤分析，使用了一種新穎的、經專家驗證的錯誤類型學。我們的結果揭示了一個關鍵的權衡：像Grok-1這樣的模型在可讀性和一致性方面表現出色，但在細緻的法律準確性上妥協，而像Claude 3 Opus這樣的模型則獲得了高準確性分數，卻掩蓋了大量微妙但關鍵的推理錯誤。錯誤分析指出了\textit{不正確的例子}和\textit{誤解}是最常見的失敗，確認了當前大型語言模型的主要挑戰不是總結，而是受控的、準確的法律推理。通過將定量基準與定性深入分析相結合，我們的工作提供了對法律應用中大型語言模型的全面且可行的評估。

##### **SwanNLP at SemEval-2026 Task 5: An LLM-based Framework for Plausibility Scoring in Narrative Word Sense Disambiguation**

Recent advances in language models have substantially improved Natural Language Understanding (NLU). ##### **Beyond Distribution Sharpening: The Importance of Task Rewards**
2604.16259v1 by Sarthak Mittal, Leo Gagnon, Guillaume Lajoie

Frontier models have demonstrated exceptional capabilities following the integration of task-reward-based reinforcement learning (RL) into their training pipelines, enabling systems to evolve from pure reasoning models into sophisticated agents. However, debate persists regarding whether RL genuinely instills new skills within a base model or merely sharpens its existing distribution to elicit latent capabilities. To address this dichotomy, we present an explicit comparison between distribution sharpening and task-reward-based learning, utilizing RL as a tool to implement both paradigms. Our analysis reveals the inherent limitations of distribution sharpening, demonstrating from first principles how and why the optima can be unfavorable and the approach fundamentally unstable. Furthermore, our experiments using Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct, Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct and Qwen3-4B-Instruct-2507 on math datasets confirm that sharpening yields limited gains, whereas incorporating task-based reward signal can greatly help achieve robust performance improvements and stable learning.

摘要：前沿模型在將基於任務獎勵的強化學習 (RL) 整合進其訓練流程後，展現了卓越的能力，使系統能夠從純粹的推理模型演變為複雜的代理。<lb/>然而，關於 RL 是否真正為基礎模型注入新技能，或僅僅是加強其現有分佈以引發潛在能力的辯論仍在持續。<lb/>為了解決這一二元對立，我們提出了基於分佈加強和基於任務獎勵學習的明確比較，利用 RL 作為工具來實現這兩種範式。<lb/>我們的分析揭示了分佈加強的固有限制，從基本原則展示了最優解為何可能不理想以及該方法根本不穩定。<lb/>此外，我們在數學數據集上使用 Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct、Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct 和 Qwen3-4B-Instruct-2507 的實驗確認，加強僅產生有限的增益，而納入基於任務的獎勵信號則能大大幫助實現穩健的性能提升和穩定的學習。

##### **Characterising LLM-Generated Competency Questions: a Cross-Domain Empirical Study using Open and Closed Models**
2604.16258v1 by Reham Alharbi, Valentina Tamma, Terry R. Payne, Jacopo de Berardinis

Competency Questions (CQs) are a cornerstone of requirement elicitation in ontology engineering. CQs represent requirements as a set of natural language questions that an ontology should satisfy; they are traditionally modelled by ontology engineers together with domain experts as part of a human-centred, manual elicitation process. The use of Generative AI automates CQ creation at scale, therefore democratising the process of generation, widening stakeholder engagement, and ultimately broadening access to ontology engineering. However, given the large and heterogeneous landscape of LLMs, varying in dimensions such as parameter scale, task and domain specialisation, and accessibility, it is crucial to characterise and understand the intrinsic, observable properties of the CQs they produce (e.g., readability, structural complexity) through a systematic, cross-domain analysis. This paper introduces a set of quantitative measures for the systematic comparison of CQs across multiple dimensions. Using CQs generated from well defined use cases and scenarios, we identify their salient properties, including readability, relevance with respect to the input text and structural complexity of the generated questions. We conduct our experiments over a set of use cases and requirements using a range of LLMs, including both open (KimiK2-1T, LLama3.1-8B, LLama3.2-3B) and closed models (Gemini 2.5 Pro, GPT 4.1). Our analysis demonstrates that LLM performance reflects distinct generation profiles shaped by the use case.

摘要：能力問題 (CQs) 是本體工程中需求引出的一個基石。<lb/>CQs 以一組自然語言問題的形式表示需求，這些問題是本體應滿足的；它們通常由本體工程師與領域專家共同建模，作為以人為中心的手動引出過程的一部分。<lb/>生成式 AI 的使用使得 CQ 的創建能夠大規模自動化，從而使生成過程民主化，擴大利益相關者的參與，最終擴大對本體工程的訪問。<lb/>然而，考慮到大型語言模型 (LLMs) 的龐大且異質的格局，這些模型在參數規模、任務和領域專業化以及可訪問性等方面各不相同，因此通過系統的跨領域分析來表徵和理解它們所生成的 CQs 的內在可觀察屬性（例如可讀性、結構複雜性）至關重要。<lb/>本文介紹了一組定量衡量標準，用於在多個維度上系統地比較 CQs。<lb/>通過使用從明確定義的用例和場景中生成的 CQs，我們識別出它們的顯著特徵，包括可讀性、與輸入文本的相關性以及生成問題的結構複雜性。<lb/>我們在一組用例和需求上進行實驗，使用多種 LLM，包括開放模型（KimiK2-1T、LLama3.1-8B、LLama3.2-3B）和封閉模型（Gemini 2.5 Pro、GPT 4.1）。<lb/>我們的分析表明，LLM 的性能反映了由用例塑造的不同生成特徵。

##### **Do Vision-Language Models Truly Perform Vision Reasoning? A Rigorous Study of the Modality Gap**
2604.16256v1 by Yige Xu, Yongjie Wang, Zizhuo Wu, Kaisong Song, Jun Lin, Zhiqi Shen

Reasoning in vision-language models (VLMs) has recently attracted significant attention due to its broad applicability across diverse downstream tasks. However, it remains unclear whether the superior performance of VLMs stems from genuine vision-grounded reasoning or relies predominantly on the reasoning capabilities of their textual backbones. To systematically measure this, we introduce CrossMath, a novel multimodal reasoning benchmark designed for controlled cross-modal comparisons. Specifically, we construct each problem in text-only, image-only, and image+text formats guaranteeing identical task-relevant information, verified by human annotators. This rigorous alignment effectively isolates modality-specific reasoning differences while eliminating confounding factors such as information mismatch. Extensive evaluation of state-of-the-art VLMs reveals a consistent phenomenon: a substantial performance gap between textual and visual reasoning. Notably, VLMs excel with text-only inputs, whereas incorporating visual data (image+text) frequently degrades performance compared to the text-only baseline. These findings indicate that current VLMs conduct reasoning primarily in the textual space, with limited genuine reliance on visual evidence. To mitigate this limitation, we curate a CrossMath training set for VLM fine-tuning. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that fine-tuning on this training set significantly boosts reasoning performance across all individual and joint modalities, while yielding robust gains on two general visual reasoning tasks. Source code is available at https://github.com/xuyige/CrossMath.

摘要：視覺-語言模型（VLMs）中的推理最近因其在多樣下游任務中的廣泛應用而受到重大關注。<lb/>然而，目前尚不清楚 VLMs 的卓越性能是否源於真正的視覺基礎推理，或主要依賴於其文本骨幹的推理能力。<lb/>為了系統性地測量這一點，我們引入了 CrossMath，一個新穎的多模態推理基準，旨在進行受控的跨模態比較。<lb/>具體而言，我們構建了每個問題的文本僅、圖像僅和圖像+文本格式，保證相同的任務相關信息，並經過人工標註者的驗證。<lb/>這種嚴格的對齊有效地隔離了模態特定的推理差異，同時消除了信息不匹配等混淆因素。<lb/>對最先進的 VLMs 的廣泛評估顯示出一個一致的現象：文本推理和視覺推理之間存在顯著的性能差距。<lb/>值得注意的是，VLMs 在僅使用文本輸入時表現優異，而引入視覺數據（圖像+文本）通常會使性能相較於僅使用文本的基準下降。<lb/>這些發現表明，目前的 VLMs 主要在文本空間中進行推理，對視覺證據的真正依賴有限。<lb/>為了減輕這一限制，我們為 VLM 微調策劃了一個 CrossMath 訓練集。<lb/>實證評估表明，在這個訓練集上進行微調顯著提升了所有單一和聯合模態的推理性能，同時在兩個通用視覺推理任務上獲得了穩健的增益。<lb/>源代碼可在 https://github.com/xuyige/CrossMath 獲得。

##### **Joint-Centric Dual Contrastive Alignment with Structure-Preserving and Information-Balanced Regularization**
2604.16247v1 by Habibeh Naderi, Behrouz Haji Soleimani, Stan Matwin

We propose HILBERT (HIerarchical Long-sequence Balanced Embedding with Reciprocal contrastive Training), a cross-attentive multimodal framework for learning document-level audio-text representations from long, segmented sequences in low-resource data settings. HILBERT leverages frozen pre-trained speech and language encoders to extract segment-level features, which are aggregated via cross-modal attention and self-attentive pooling to form modality-specific document representations and a joint cross-attentive embedding. To align modalities while preserving modality-specific structure under severe audio-text dimensional imbalance, we introduce a reciprocal dual contrastive objective that simultaneously aligns audio-to-joint and text-to-joint representations, rather than directly contrasting audio and text alone. Two auxiliary regularizers further stabilize long-sequence fusion: a Centered Kernel Alignment (CKA) loss that preserves structural consistency between each modality and the joint embedding, and a mutual information balancing loss that prevents dominance of a single modality by equalizing information flow from audio and text into the joint space. For downstream prediction, HILBERT employs a Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) classifier over concatenated audio, text, and joint representations to accommodate heterogeneous label regimes. Extensive evaluation across multiple audio-text backbone combinations demonstrates that HILBERT learns semantically meaningful long-sequence representations and achieves superior performance on highly imbalanced multi-class settings.

摘要：我們提出了HILBERT（HIerarchical Long-sequence Balanced Embedding with Reciprocal contrastive Training），這是一個跨注意力的多模態框架，用於在低資源數據環境中從長的分段序列學習文檔級音頻-文本表示。HILBERT利用凍結的預訓練語音和語言編碼器來提取段級特徵，這些特徵通過跨模態注意力和自注意力池化進行聚合，以形成模態特定的文檔表示和聯合跨注意力嵌入。為了在嚴重的音頻-文本維度不平衡下對齊模態，同時保持模態特定結構，我們引入了一個互惠的雙重對比目標，該目標同時對齊音頻到聯合和文本到聯合的表示，而不是僅僅直接對比音頻和文本。兩個輔助正則化器進一步穩定長序列融合：一個中心核對齊（CKA）損失，保持每個模態與聯合嵌入之間的結構一致性，以及一個互信息平衡損失，通過平衡音頻和文本進入聯合空間的信息流來防止單一模態的主導。對於下游預測，HILBERT在串接的音頻、文本和聯合表示上使用混合專家（MoE）分類器，以適應異質標籤範疇。在多個音頻-文本主幹組合上的廣泛評估表明，HILBERT學習了語義上有意義的長序列表示，並在高度不平衡的多類設置中實現了卓越的性能。

##### **Detecting and Suppressing Reward Hacking with Gradient Fingerprints**
2604.16242v1 by Songtao Wang, Quang Hieu Pham, Fangcong Yin, Xinpeng Wang, Jocelyn Qiaochu Chen, Greg Durrett, Xi Ye

Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) typically optimizes for outcome rewards without imposing constraints on intermediate reasoning. This leaves training susceptible to reward hacking, where models exploit loopholes (e.g., spurious patterns in training data) in the reward function to achieve high scores without solving the intended task. These reward-hacking behaviors are often implicit, as the intermediate chain-of-thought (CoT) may appear plausible on the surface, limiting the effectiveness of purely text-based monitoring. We propose Gradient Fingerprint (GRIFT), a method for detecting reward hacking using models' internal computations. Given a prompt and a model-generated CoT, GRIFT computes gradients of the CoT conditioned on the prompt and compresses them into a compact representation, which is then used to assess whether the CoT reflects reward hacking behavior. Across verifiable reasoning benchmarks spanning math, code, and logical reasoning, GRIFT substantially outperforms strong baselines, including CoT Monitor and TRACE, achieving over 25% relative improvement in detecting reward hacking behavior. Moreover, integrating GRIFT into the rejection fine-tuning pipeline for reasoning tasks reduces reward hacking and improves performance on the true task objective. Our results highlight a promising direction of leveraging gradient level representations for assessing the quality of CoT reasoning traces. Our code is available at: https://github.com/songtao-x/reward_hack.

摘要：強化學習與可驗證獎勵（RLVR）通常優化結果獎勵，而不對中間推理施加約束。這使得訓練容易受到獎勵黑客行為的影響，模型利用獎勵函數中的漏洞（例如，訓練數據中的虛假模式）來獲得高分，而不解決預期的任務。這些獎勵黑客行為通常是隱性的，因為中間的思考鏈（CoT）表面上可能看起來合理，這限制了純文本監控的有效性。我們提出了梯度指紋（GRIFT），這是一種使用模型內部計算來檢測獎勵黑客的方法。給定一個提示和模型生成的 CoT，GRIFT 計算基於提示的 CoT 的梯度，並將其壓縮為緊湊的表示，然後用於評估該 CoT 是否反映獎勵黑客行為。在涵蓋數學、代碼和邏輯推理的可驗證推理基準上，GRIFT 顯著超越了強基準，包括 CoT 監控和 TRACE，在檢測獎勵黑客行為方面實現了超過 25% 的相對改進。此外，將 GRIFT 整合到推理任務的拒絕微調流程中可以減少獎勵黑客行為，並提高在真實任務目標上的性能。我們的結果突顯了利用梯度級表示來評估 CoT 推理痕跡質量的有前景方向。我們的代碼可在以下地址獲得：https://github.com/songtao-x/reward_hack。

##### **BAGEL: Benchmarking Animal Knowledge Expertise in Language Models**
2604.16241v1 by Jiacheng Shen, Masato Hagiwara, Milad Alizadeh, Ellen Gilsenan-McMahon, Marius Miron, David Robinson, Emmanuel Chemla, Sara Keen, Gagan Narula, Mathieu Laurière, Matthieu Geist, Olivier Pietquin

Large language models have shown strong performance on broad-domain knowledge and reasoning benchmarks, but it remains unclear how well language models handle specialized animal-related knowledge under a unified closed-book evaluation protocol. We introduce BAGEL, a benchmark for evaluating animal knowledge expertise in language models. BAGEL is constructed from diverse scientific and reference sources, including bioRxiv, Global Biotic Interactions, Xeno-canto, and Wikipedia, using a combination of curated examples and automatically generated closed-book question-answer pairs. The benchmark covers multiple aspects of animal knowledge, including taxonomy, morphology, habitat, behavior, vocalization, geographic distribution, and species interactions. By focusing on closed-book evaluation, BAGEL measures animal-related knowledge of models without external retrieval at inference time. BAGEL further supports fine-grained analysis across source domains, taxonomic groups, and knowledge categories, enabling a more precise characterization of model strengths and systematic failure modes. Our benchmark provides a new testbed for studying domain-specific knowledge generalization in language models and for improving their reliability in biodiversity-related applications.

摘要：大型語言模型在廣泛領域的知識和推理基準上表現出色，但尚不清楚語言模型在統一的閉卷評估協議下如何處理專門的動物相關知識。我們介紹了BAGEL，一個用於評估語言模型中動物知識專業性的基準。BAGEL是從多種科學和參考來源構建的，包括bioRxiv、Global Biotic Interactions、Xeno-canto和維基百科，使用精心策劃的示例和自動生成的閉卷問答對的組合。該基準涵蓋了動物知識的多個方面，包括分類學、形態學、棲息地、行為、聲音、地理分佈和物種互動。通過專注於閉卷評估，BAGEL在推理時不依賴外部檢索來測量模型的動物相關知識。BAGEL還支持跨來源領域、分類群和知識類別的細緻分析，使模型的優勢和系統性失敗模式能夠更精確地表徵。我們的基準為研究語言模型中的領域特定知識泛化以及提高其在生物多樣性相關應用中的可靠性提供了一個新的測試平台。

##### **Optimizing Korean-Centric LLMs via Token Pruning**
2604.16235v1 by Hoyeol Kim, Hyeonwoo Kim

This paper presents a systematic benchmark of state-of-the-art multilingual large language models (LLMs) adapted via token pruning - a compression technique that eliminates tokens and embedding parameters corresponding to languages irrelevant to the target application. Focusing on Korean-centric natural language processing (NLP) tasks, we evaluate architectures including Qwen3, Gemma-3, Llama-3, and Aya across three vocabulary configurations: Original, English-Korean (EnKo), and English-Korean-Chinese (EnKoZh). Performance is assessed using established benchmarks for general aptitude, cultural literacy, instruction following, and machine translation. Our findings indicate that token pruning significantly improves generation stability by eliminating language confusion, and in the case of machine translation, frequently enhances performance on Korean-specific tasks. While instruction-following capabilities display architecture-dependent variance linked to latent cross-lingual representations, the significant reduction in vocabulary size validates token pruning as a highly effective optimization strategy for memory-constrained, domain-specific deployments, despite modest gains in inference latency.

摘要：這篇論文呈現了一個系統性的基準測試，針對通過標記修剪調整的最先進多語言大型語言模型（LLMs）進行評估——這是一種壓縮技術，旨在消除與目標應用無關的語言所對應的標記和嵌入參數。<lb/>專注於以韓語為中心的自然語言處理（NLP）任務，我們評估了包括Qwen3、Gemma-3、Llama-3和Aya在內的架構，並針對三種詞彙配置進行評估：原始、英韓（EnKo）和英韓中文（EnKoZh）。<lb/>性能評估使用了針對一般能力、文化素養、指令跟隨和機器翻譯的既定基準。<lb/>我們的研究結果表明，標記修剪通過消除語言混淆顯著提高了生成的穩定性，並且在機器翻譯的情況下，經常增強了在韓語特定任務上的表現。<lb/>雖然指令跟隨能力顯示出與潛在跨語言表徵相關的架構依賴性變異，但詞彙大小的顯著減少驗證了標記修剪作為一種對於內存受限、特定領域部署的高度有效優化策略，儘管推理延遲的增益較為有限。

##### **A Two-Stage, Object-Centric Deep Learning Framework for Robust Exam Cheating Detection**
2604.16234v1 by Van-Truong Le, Le-Khanh Nguyen, Trong-Doanh Nguyen

Academic integrity continues to face the persistent challenge of examination cheating. Traditional invigilation relies on human observation, which is inefficient, costly, and prone to errors at scale. Although some existing AI-powered monitoring systems have been deployed and trusted, many lack transparency or require multi-layered architectures to achieve the desired performance. To overcome these challenges, we propose an improvement over a simple two-stage framework for exam cheating detection that integrates object detection and behavioral analysis using well-known technologies. First, the state-of-the-art YOLOv8n model is used to localize students in exam-room images. Each detected region is cropped and preprocessed, then classified by a fine-tuned RexNet-150 model as either normal or cheating behavior. The system is trained on a dataset compiled from 10 independent sources with a total of 273,897 samples, achieving 0.95 accuracy, 0.94 recall, 0.96 precision, and 0.95 F1-score - a 13\% increase over a baseline accuracy of 0.82 in video-based cheating detection. In addition, with an average inference time of 13.9 ms per sample, the proposed approach demonstrates robustness and scalability for deployment in large-scale environments. Beyond the technical contribution, the AI-assisted monitoring system also addresses ethical concerns by ensuring that final outcomes are delivered privately to individual students after the examination, for example, via personal email. This prevents public exposure or shaming and offers students an opportunity to reflect on their behavior. For further improvement, it is possible to incorporate additional factors, such as audio data and consecutive frames, to achieve greater accuracy. This study provides a foundation for developing real-time, scalable, ethical, and open-source solutions.

##### **Neuro-Symbolic ODE Discovery with Latent Grammar Flow**
2604.16232v1 by Karin Yu, Eleni Chatzi, Georgios Kissas

Understanding natural and engineered systems often relies on symbolic formulations, such as differential equations, which provide interpretability and transferability beyond black-box models.
  We introduce Latent Grammar Flow (LGF), a neuro-symbolic generative framework for discovering ordinary differential equations from data. LGF embeds equations as grammar-based representations into a discrete latent space and forces semantically similar equations to be positioned closer together with a behavioural loss. Then, a discrete flow model guides the sampling process to recursively generate candidate equations that best fit the observed data. Domain knowledge and constraints, such as stability, can be either embedded into the rules or used as conditional predictors.

##### **Beyond Surface Statistics: Robust Conformal Prediction for LLMs via Internal Representations**
2604.16217v1 by Yanli Wang, Peng Kuang, Xiaoyu Han, Kaidi Xu, Haohan Wang

Large language models are increasingly deployed in settings where reliability matters, yet output-level uncertainty signals such as token probabilities, entropy, and self-consistency can become brittle under calibration--deployment mismatch. Conformal prediction provides finite-sample validity under exchangeability, but its practical usefulness depends on the quality of the nonconformity score. We propose a conformal framework for LLM question answering that uses internal representations rather than output-facing statistics: specifically, we introduce Layer-Wise Information (LI) scores, which measure how conditioning on the input reshapes predictive entropy across model depth, and use them as nonconformity scores within a standard split conformal pipeline. Across closed-ended and open-domain QA benchmarks, with the clearest gains under cross-domain shift, our method achieves a better validity--efficiency trade-off than strong text-level baselines while maintaining competitive in-domain reliability at the same nominal risk level. These results suggest that internal representations can provide more informative conformal scores when surface-level uncertainty is unstable under distribution shift.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越多地被部署在可靠性至關重要的環境中，然而，像是標記概率、熵和自一致性等輸出級不確定性信號在校準與部署不匹配的情況下可能變得脆弱。符合預測在可交換性下提供有限樣本的有效性，但其實際有用性取決於不符合性分數的質量。我們提出了一個用於 LLM 問答的符合框架，該框架使用內部表示而非面向輸出的統計數據：具體來說，我們引入了層級信息 (LI) 分數，這些分數衡量在模型深度上如何根據輸入的條件重塑預測熵，並將其用作標準分割符合管道中的不符合性分數。在封閉式和開放領域的 QA 基準測試中，我們的方法在跨領域轉移下獲得了明顯的增益，實現了比強文本級基準更好的有效性與效率的權衡，同時在相同名義風險水平下保持競爭性的域內可靠性。這些結果表明，當表面級不確定性在分佈轉移下不穩定時，內部表示可以提供更具信息性的符合分數。

##### **ChemGraph-XANES: An Agentic Framework for XANES Simulation and Analysis**
2604.16205v1 by Vitor F. Grizzi, Thang Duc Pham, Luke N. Pretzie, Jiayi Xu, Murat Keceli, Cong Liu

Computational X-ray absorption near-edge structure (XANES) is widely used to probe local coordination environments, oxidation states, and electronic structure in chemically complex systems. However, the use of computational XANES at scale is constrained more by workflow complexity than by the underlying simulation method itself. To address this challenge, we present ChemGraph-XANES, an agentic framework for automated XANES simulation and analysis that unifies natural-language task specification, structure acquisition, FDMNES input generation, task-parallel execution, spectral normalization, and provenance-aware data curation. Built on ASE, FDMNES, Parsl, and a LangGraph/LangChain-based tool interface, the framework exposes XANES workflow operations as typed Python tools that can be orchestrated by large language model (LLM) agents. In multi-agent mode, a retrieval-augmented expert agent consults the FDMNES manual to ground parameter selection, while executor agents translate user requests into structured tool calls. We demonstrate documentation-grounded parameter retrieval and show that the same workflow supports both explicit structure-file inputs and chemistry-level natural-language requests. Because independent XANES calculations are naturally task-parallel, the framework is well suited for high-throughput deployment on high-performance computing (HPC) systems, enabling scalable XANES database generation for downstream analysis and machine-learning applications. ChemGraph-XANES thus provides a reproducible and extensible workflow layer for physics-based XANES simulation, spectral curation, and agent-compatible computational spectroscopy.

摘要：計算X射線吸收邊緣結構（XANES）廣泛用於探測化學複雜系統中的局部配位環境、氧化態和電子結構。<lb/>然而，計算XANES的規模使用受到工作流程複雜性的限制，而非底層模擬方法本身。<lb/>為了解決這一挑戰，我們提出了ChemGraph-XANES，這是一個自動化XANES模擬和分析的代理框架，統一了自然語言任務規範、結構獲取、FDMNES輸入生成、任務並行執行、光譜正規化和來源感知數據管理。<lb/>該框架基於ASE、FDMNES、Parsl和基於LangGraph/LangChain的工具介面，將XANES工作流程操作暴露為類型化的Python工具，這些工具可以被大型語言模型（LLM）代理協調。<lb/>在多代理模式下，一個增強檢索的專家代理諮詢FDMNES手冊以確定參數選擇，而執行代理則將用戶請求轉換為結構化工具調用。<lb/>我們展示了基於文檔的參數檢索，並顯示相同的工作流程支持明確的結構文件輸入和化學層級的自然語言請求。<lb/>由於獨立的XANES計算自然上是任務並行的，該框架非常適合在高性能計算（HPC）系統上進行高通量部署，從而實現可擴展的XANES數據庫生成，以供下游分析和機器學習應用。<lb/>因此，ChemGraph-XANES為基於物理的XANES模擬、光譜管理和代理兼容的計算光譜學提供了一個可重現和可擴展的工作流程層。

##### **Synthetic data in cryptocurrencies using generative models**
2604.16182v1 by André Saimon S. Sousa, Otto Pires, Frank Acasiete, Oscar M. Granados, Valéria Loureiro da Silva, Hugo Saba

Data plays a fundamental role in consolidating markets, services, and products in the digital financial ecosystem. However, the use of real data, especially in the financial context, can lead to privacy risks and access restrictions, affecting institutions, research, and modeling processes. The approach is based on Conditional Generative Adversarial Networks (CGANs), combining an LSTM-type recurrent generator and an MLP discriminator to produce statistically consistent synthetic data. The experiments consider different crypto-assets and demonstrate that the model is capable of reproducing relevant temporal patterns, preserving market trends and dynamics. The generation of synthetic series through GANs is an efficient alternative for simulating financial data, showing potential for applications such as market behavior analysis and anomaly detection, with lower computational cost compared to more complex generative approaches.

##### **MARCH: Multi-Agent Radiology Clinical Hierarchy for CT Report Generation**
2604.16175v1 by Yi Lin, Yihao Ding, Yonghui Wu, Yifan Peng

Automated 3D radiology report generation often suffers from clinical hallucinations and a lack of the iterative verification found in human practice. While recent Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have advanced the field, they typically operate as monolithic "black-box" systems without the collaborative oversight characteristic of clinical workflows. To address these challenges, we propose MARCH (Multi-Agent Radiology Clinical Hierarchy), a multi-agent framework that emulates the professional hierarchy of radiology departments and assigns specialized roles to distinct agents. MARCH utilizes a Resident Agent for initial drafting with multi-scale CT feature extraction, multiple Fellow Agents for retrieval-augmented revision, and an Attending Agent that orchestrates an iterative, stance-based consensus discourse to resolve diagnostic discrepancies.
